Ivyo abacukuzi bavumbuye vyerekana ko hariho **ivyambu vy’ubudandaji n’ibibanza vy’ubudandaji mu bisagara vya Mezopotamiya kuva mu kinjana ca kabiri**. Ivyo bikorwa remezo biremeza ko hariho amasoko atunganijwe, naho nyene ukuntu akora nyavyo biguma biharirwa.



Karl Polanyi, mu ntango yari ashidikanya ku kuba hariho uburyo nyakuri bwo gukora isoko mu bihe vya kera, yarashize ahabona ikibanza ciwe mu kwemera yuko yoba yarasuzuguye ukuntu isoko ry’ubudandaji ryatangura guseruka. Ukwo gutera imbere kw’ubwenge kwerekana ukuntu vyari bigoye gusobanura uburyo bwa kera bw’ubutunzi, aho ugusubira gusangira inzego, uguhanahana, n’ugucuruza kw’isoko vyari bikiri bito vyari bifatanye.



### Siparita na Atene



Igereranyo riri hagati ya Siparita n’i Atene ryerekana neza isano riri hagati y’urutonde rw’amahera n’imitunganirize y’imibano. **Sparta igereranya akarorero k’igihugu gifise ubukuru bukomeye bwanka n’ibigirankana gukoresha amahera**, mu gihe Atene yateye imbere ubutunzi bw’amahera buteye imbere kugira ngo buherekezwe n’uburyo bwayo bwa demokarasi.



Ukwanka amahera kw’Abaspartan ntikwari kwibonekeza, ahubwo kwari **inzego n’ingengabitekerezo**. Abarongozi b’i Spartan batinya ko amahera yoshobora kwonona agaciro k’igisirikare n’ak’abanyagihugu, bagahitamwo uburyo bushingiye ku kwizigirana ata guca ku ruhande hagati y’abanyagihugu.



Kugira ngo Sparta ntibakoreshe amahera, yakoresheje **ivyuma biremerera kandi bidakora**, ivyo bikaba vyerekana mu buryo buteye ubwoba ko batahura neza kamere z’amahera (ugucapura, gutwara, gukomera) bariko baragerageza gukuraho.



### Imipaka y'Icitegererezo c'Ukurwanya Amahera



Ishirahamwe ry’Abaspartan ryerekana inzitizi z’umubare wa **Dunbar** zikoreshwa ku rugero rw’imibano. **Mu kwanka amahera nk’uburyo bwo guhinduranya ataco buvuze, Sparta yariciriye urubanza rwo guhagarika umuryango wayo w’abanyagihugu ku mubare mutoyi w’abanyagihugu bashobora kugumana imigenderanire y’ukwizigirana ata guca ku ruhande**. Aba homoioi (abanyagihugu bo muri Siparita) bari 1 kw’ijana gusa vy’abantu bose, bakikujwe n’ibihumbi vy’abahilote (abaja).



Iryo shirahamwe, mu ntango ryari isoko y’ubumwe budasanzwe bw’igisirikare, ryagaragaye ko ridakomeye mu mibumbe. **Intambara ya Leuctres (371 BC) yerekanye aho iyo nzira igarukira**: ukubura ubuzima kwasenyuye ataco bimaze imibano y’Abanyasipani, bituma urugero rwabo rw’ubutekerezi rusenyuka.



Ibisagara bihiganwa (Atene, Korinto, Tebesi), bifise uburyo bw’amahera buteye imbere, **bigumye bifise ubutunzi butunze, bukomeye cane**, bishobora gusubiza inyuma ivyo abantu bahomvye biciye mu gusubira kwubaka ubutunzi no kwimukira mu bindi bihugu.



### Umuntu ku giti ciwe n'ukwizigira kw'inzego



Ivyo aba Spartan baciyemwo birerekana **ingorane ziri mu kibano gishingiye gusa ku kwizigirana hagati y’abantu** aho gushingira ku buryo bw’inzego butagira aho bugarukira. Naho nyene iyo nzira yatuma haba ubumwe bukomeye mu kibano, yatumye abantu bashobora gushikirwa n’ingorane z’imibare y’abantu.



Mu gushoboza amafaranga atamenyekana kandi ata muntu, amahera atanga ubushobozi bwo kwihangana burengeye ubw’abandi. Bituma haba ukwaguka kw’imibano birenze imipaka y’ukwizigirana gutaziguye, bigatuma haba uguhinduranya amafaranga y’amahanga n’iterambere ry’ubutunzi.



### Ivyiyumviro vy’Abanyainca, Ubutunzi butagira Amahera



Ubwami bw’Abainca buratanga ikintu giteye ubwoba giteye ubwoba: **ubutekerezi bufise ubutunzi bwinshi cane bw’inzahabu ariko ata n’uburyo bw’amahera**. Cokimwe na Sparta, iyo nzira yari ishingiye ku ntumbero ikomeye y’ubukuru n’imigambi ihurikiye hamwe, ariko yerekanye ko ishobora gushikirwa n’abanyagihugu bafise ubutunzi bw’amahera bushobora guhinduka.



Ukwo gusenyuka kw’imiterere y’imibumbe irwanya amafaranga mu gihe c’imibano y’amahera ni ikintu gisubira inyuma mu mateka, kikaba kigaragaza ko **ukwanga amahera mu nzego, kure y’ugukomeza ubumwe bw’abantu, bishobora gutuma amateka agoyagoya mu buryo buteye ubwoba** mu gihe c’ingorane zo hanze n’ihinduka ry’amateka.



Isesengura ry’ivyo bigereranyo vy’amateka ryerekana ko amahera, uretse igikorwa cayo co guhinduranya, ari ikimenyetso kandi yorosha ugusobanuka kw’imibano, bikaba bishoboza amateka kurenga imipaka iterwa n’imigenderanire itaziguye hagati y’abantu.



# Ivuka ry'amahera yacuzwe .


<partId>232e365a-8c3b-11f0-b276-b3ab70d1a5a1</partId>



## Uguseruka kw'ibiceri


<chapterId>40ed3414-3066-57bd-bc1b-617ad0a354e0</chapterId>


:::video id=1d6834c4-98a3-43fe-ba80-04be51b0486e:::

Ubu twashitse ku ntumbero nyamukuru y’ikibazo: ukuntu ibiceri bisa. Nshimikiye kw’ijambo ‘igiceri’ aha kuko twabonye mu bice vya kera ko amahera canke uburyo bwo gukoresha amahera bwariho cane mu mateka yabanjirije abantu b’i Lidiya, Abagiriki n’Abaperesi. Biragaragara neza, nibwira, ku vyo twamaze kubona. Iki gice rero kigenewe ukuza kw’ibiceri vy’amahera vy’ukuri kandi gifise umutwe uvuga ngo: *Uguseruka kw’ibiceri*.



### Inkomoko y'ibiceri vyo muri Lidiya no muri Iyoniya



Kugira ngo ntangire iki gice, ndashaka kubaha igice c’igitabu ca Glyn Davies, Amateka y’Amahera, hano nyene.



*Igice kimwe co mu gitabu Amateka y'Amahera: Kuva Kera Gushika Ubu canditswe na Glyn Davies:*



> Kuva aho yavukiye i Lidiya n’i Iyoniya, ubumenyi n’ugukoresha ibiceri vyarakwiragiye ningoga mu buseruko mu bwami bw’Ubuperesi no mu burengero biciye mu bindi birwa vya Yoniya n’ivya Égée gushika mu Bugiriki buhambaye, hanyuma bishika mu bihugu vyari vyarigaruriye mu burengero, canecane muri Sicile. Yarakwiragiye kandi mu buraruko gushika muri Makedoniya, muri Trasiya no mu Kiyaga Cirabura, ariko mu Misiri yemerewe gusa igice, ata co yipfuza kandi itevye.

Nsanga bishimishije kuvuga aha ko muri Misiri, babandanije gupima ibiceri haciye igihe kirekire ubuhinga bwo gukora ibiceri buje. Ngira ngo ivyo ni ngirakamaro kubimenya. Ivyo bivugwa birabandanya:



> Mu buryo nk’ubwo, Ubutaliyano bwo mu gihugu nyamukuru na bwo nyene mu ntango bwari buteye buhoro cane mu kwemera ibintu bishasha vy’ubutunzi vy’Abagiriki, bitandukanye n’ingene Sicile yavyemeye vyihuta.

*Uretse ivyo bihugu bibiri bifise aho bigarukira (Ubutaliyano bwo mu Butaliyano na Misiri yo Hasi), ikoreshwa ry’ibiceri ryarakwiragiye cane mu bihugu bikikije ikiyaga Mediterane hagati n’ubusereko, be no mu Bwami buhambaye kandi bwariko burakura bw’Ubuperesi, kuva muri Mezopotamiya **gushika mu Buhindi. muri ico gihe, ataco bimaze mu bijanye n’iterambere ry’Abashinwa canke ry’Abaludiya. Utitaye ku kuba Ubuhinde bwari bwateguye amahera yabwo bwite, ukuntu Ubuhinde n’Uburasirazuba bwa hafi bwariko burakorana cane vyatumye amafaranga y’Abahindi ahindurwa ata guca ku ruhande n’ubuhinga bwa Lidiya n’Ubugiriki, ubwa mbere biciye mu Bwami bw’Ubuperesi hanyuma mu Bwami bwa Makedoniya* (n’ivyo Alegizandere Mukuru na se wiwe banesheje).



*Kubera izo mpamvu, ingaruka zitaziguye z’ubuhinga bwose bw’abanyagihugu b’Abahindi bwo guhingura amahera zari nto cane, ugereranije n’akamaro gakomeye cane k’ubuhinga bwo guhingura amahera bwigenga bugaragara bw’Ubushinwa mu buseruko, mbere n’iterambere ry’Abanyalidiya n’Abagiriki mu burengero*



### Ugukwiragizwa kw'ibibanza n'uguhindura akarere



![image](assets/rn/005.webp)



Kugira ngo tugaragaze ico kiringo mu buryo buboneka, aha hejuru hari igiceri co mu karere kamwe ko mu Buhindi, akarere ka Bactria, kakaba kari hafi y’uburengero bw’izinga ry’Ubuhindi, hafi y’igihugu ca Afghanistan. Muri ako karere, hariho ibiceri bishobora kuba vyari vyahumekewe n’ibiceri vy’Abagiriki vyerekana kimwe mu bintu vyabo vy’ubwami.




## Abaludiya n’Abaperesi .


<chapterId>eb802ab8-8ffd-5b25-907f-8944f120ed14</chapterId>


:::video id=f151eb42-5ff3-4ca1-9af1-1ae2a5e051c0:::

### Ibiceri vya mbere vy’umuyagankuba vy’i Lidiya



Ko tutashobora gutandukanya ukuntu ibiceri bisa n’ivyo Lidiya n’Abaperesi, reka tugende kuri ico gice c’isi kiri mu buseruko bw’Ubugiriki, uno musi kikaba ari co Turukiya. Ibiceri vya mbere vyabonetse mu Burengero vyabonetse nko hagati mu kinjana ca 7 imbere ya Kristu, mu turere twa Lidiya na Ioniya, turi muri Turukiya y’ubu. Ni nko mu myaka ya 650 gushika kuri 600 imbere ya Kristu aho ico kintu gishasha c’ishimikiro cabonetse, hakaba hariho ibintu bihambaye vy’ubucukuzi nk’ibiceri vya mbere vyabonetse mu rusengero rwa Aritemi i Efeso, vyabonetse nko mu myaka ya 600 imbere ya Kristu. Ivyo biceri vya kera vyari bikozwe mu gikoresho citwa electrum, kikaba ari ikintu gikomeye c’inzahabu n’ifeza bifise amabara y’agahama, kandi akenshi vyari bimeze nk’ibitoke, bikaba vyari bifise gusa ibimenyetso vy’ibipfunsi canke ibimenyetso vy’intango.


Hasi, urashobora kubona kimwe mu biceri vya kera cane vyo muri Lidiya, kikaba kirimwo intare ifise umuhigo wayo imbere. Ushobora kubona ikidodo canke umwobo inyuma, bamwebamwe bemera ko vyakoreshejwe kugira ngo bagerageze ubusuku bw’ico cuma no kugira ngo bamenye neza ko atari ikintu co hejuru gusa. Naho iyi ari imwe mu ngero za mbere, birahambaye kumenya ko iki gice ari kopi. Ibice vyanje vyose vy’inzahabu n’ivy’amashanyarazi ni ibishushanyo canke ivy’ukwinezereza vyo muri iki gihe, vyagenewe kunkingira gukoresha amahera yose nazigamye muri iri koraniro.


![image](assets/rn/006.webp)



Ariko kandi mfise igice c’Ubuperesi nyaco turiko turabona. Uko ni ko ivyo bipande vya mbere vyari bisa. Ni nk’ubwoko bw’igipfunsi (canke igipfunsi, mu congereza) c’icuma cari giteye ikidodo ico gihe.



Mu buryo butandukanye n’ukwemera kwakwiragiye kw’uko amahera yahinguwe kugira ngo yorohereze ubudandaji bwa misi yose no gusubirira uguhinduranya, bisa n’uko mu ntango ibiceri vya mbere vy’Abaludiya, Abakemeni n’Abagiriki bitakoreshwa mu bucuruzi buto buto. Nkako, izo nkuru z’amahera zari nyinshi cane ku buryo zitashobora gukoreshwa ku musi ku musi. Ikindi kandi, ukuntu vyagenda vyari bigarukiye mu turere turi hafi y’aho vyakorerwa.



Aha, mbona ko ari ngirakamaro kuvuga ko, naho nasomye mu bitabu vyinshi vy’ubuhinga bw’abantu, ibiceri, nk’uko namaze kubigaragaza - vyaba ivy’amashanyarazi canke iki giceri c’Ubuperesi nzosubirako mu gihe gito cane - vyari binini cane ku buryo ntashobora kugura umukate, tuvuge, buri musi. Nabonye ingereranyo zotuma twiyumvira ko bingana n’igikorwa c’umusi umwe ku murimyi canke ku musirikare, rero vyoba ari binini cane. Ni nk'ukugerageza kuriha umushahara w'umusi ku mfungurwa zawe, icayi cawe co mu gitondo canke ica sasita. Keretse ko nabonye mu bindi bikorwa ko hariho utugingo ngengabuzima dutoduto tw’ivyo bice, rero ibiceri bitobito, ivyo bishobora gutuma twiyumvira ko kumbure hariho uburyo bwo kubigura ku musi ku musi.


Rero aha, "ikimenyamenya" c'ubuhinga bw'abantu c'uko kitakoreshwa mu bucuruzi bwa misi yose, kubera ko idini canke igice cari kinini cane, ntigikomeye cane mu ciyumviro canje kuko twabonye ingero z'ibiceri bitobito, vyari gushobora gukoreshwa mu gugura kwa misi yose.



### Uruhara rwa Leta mu kurema amafaranga .



Inkomoko nyakuri y’ibiceri isa n’iyifitaniye isano n’igikorwa gitaziguye c’ibihugu. Hariho ivyiyumviro bibiri nyamukuru kuri iyo nkuru: ica mbere, c’ivyiyumviro, gihuza ijambo ry’ikigiriki ‘nomisma’ (amahera) n’‘nomos’ (amategeko), bikaba vyerekana ko amahera yari afitaniye isano n’ugushinga amategeko, bikomeza ubukuru n’imitunganirize ya politike y’ibisagara. Iciyumviro ca kabiri, gifise ukuri kuruta, cemerwa cane muri iki gihe, ni uko amahera yari uburyo bwa mbere na mbere Leta zikoresha mu kugenzura ubutunzi n’imibano. Mu kwemeza ku mugaragaro uburemere n’agaciro k’ivyuma vy’agaciro vyari muri vyo, ibihugu vyarashoboye gukoresha nabi ukuntu ivyo biceri bigenda n’agaciro, bituma habaho icizigiro n’amahera y’ugutanga amahera yihariye ku mafaranga yo mu gihugu.



Birashimishije cane kumenya ko dufise ibimenyamenya vy’ivyo. Nk’akarorero, mu biceri vy’amashanyarazi, ukwiye kumenya ko amashanyarazi kavukire mu bisanzwe ari hafi y’ibice 70% vy’inzahabu na 30% vy’ifeza. Mu biceri vya mbere twabonye kandi twabisuzumye, cane cane ibiceri vya kera vy’i Lidiya, inzahabu isa n’iyirimwo cane hafi 50 gushika kuri 55% aho kuba 70. Ivyo vyerekana ko no muri ico gihe, abatanga ibiceri bariko bagerageza kugabanya umugabane w’icuma c’agaciro kuruta, kumbure kugira ngo bashobore gutanga ibiceri vyinshi kandi bibe nk’ibifise agaciro kanini. Kandi aha, bitegerezwa kuvugwa ko vy’ukuri kuva mu gihe c’uwo Croesus rurangiranwa, nk’uko biri muri *rich as Croesus*, ivyo vyashobotse kuko kuva mu gihe ciwe niho twaronka ubuhinga bwo gutandukanya inzahabu n’ifeza.



Ivyuma vy’i Lidiya vyarahindutse cane ku ngoma y’umwami rurangiranwa yitwa Croesus (561-546 imbere ya Kristu), yari azwi cane kubera ubutunzi bwiwe bw’imigani. Muri ico gihe, Abanyaludiya baratunganije ubuhinga bwo gutandukanya inzahabu n’ifeza n’umuyagankuba, gutyo barazana ibiceri vya mbere vy’ivyuma bibiri, ni ukuvuga ibiceri vy’inzahabu n’ifeza bitandukanye.



### Ukwaguka kw'Abaperesi n'ukwemera kw'Abagiriki



Igihe bigarurira Lidiya mu mwaka w’546 imbere ya Kristu, Abaperesi b’Abakemenide baca bafata iyo nzira nshasha. Nko mu mwaka wa 500 imbere ya Kristu, ku ngoma ya Dariyo wa mbere, Abaperesi barashizeho uburyo bwabo bwo gukoresha amahera bakoresheje amadaraki y’inzahabu n’amasiglois y’ifeza, akenshi bakaba bafise igishushanyo c’umwami mu buryo bw’intambara. Ivyo biceri vy’umwami vy’Ubuperesi vyakoreshwa canecane mu turere tw’Ubwami bw’Ubuperesi twari twagizwe n’Abagiriki, maze buhorobuhoro birakwiragira, naho nyene ikoreshwa ryavyo ryagumye ridahuye, **uturere tumwetumwe, nka Misiri, twari tugikunda guhindura ivyuma bipima (bullion).**.



![image](assets/rn/007.webp)



Hejuru, urashobora gushima sigloi (canke siglos) y’ukuri y’Abaperesi. Ico gishushanyo gitoyi kirimwo umwami, naho nyene ico kinogo cari carashaje gatoyi. Siglos ni igiceri c’ifeza, gitandukanye n’igiceri c’ifeza citwa daric, kikaba cari gikozwe mu nzahabu. Abaperesi barashobora gutandukanya ivyo vyuma bibiri, maze barava ku biceri vy’umuyagankuba. Rero, barashize mu ngiro ubuhinga bwo gukoresha ivyuma bibiri, bakoresheje inzahabu n’ifeza mu gihe bagumye bafise iciyumviro kimwe c’ibiceri bikozwe mu vyuma vy’agaciro, akenshi bikaba bifise umwobo inyuma, bishoboka ko ari vyo vyo gusuzuma ivyuma birimwo.


Bisa n’uko Abagiriki baciye bafata ibiceri vyihuse kubera ko bari bafitaniye ubucuti bwa hafi n’Abanyaludiya, canecane biciye ku bihugu vy’Abagiriki vyari vyarigaruriye muri Aziya Ntoya. Abagiriki ba mbere bacuze ibiceri bashobora kuba bari abatuye i Egina hagati mu kinjana ca gatandatu imbere ya Kristu, ni bo bashizeho idarakima, uburemere bwayo bukaba butandukanye ku ntara ku yindi, kandi izina ryayo risobanura "urushinge rw'intete" canke "urushinge rw'imyampi".


Ukuroranirwa kw’ibiceri vy’Abagiriki kwari guterwa n’uko vyari vyiza mu gukora ibikorwa bihambaye, nk’ugutanga amahera y’abacangero, be n’uko vyari vyoroshe mu kwagura ubutunzi n’ivya politike vy’ibisagara. Amafaranga yaciye yihuta kuba ikintu nyamukuru mu vy’ubutunzi bw’Abagiriki, mu nyuma no mu vy’ubutunzi bw’Abaroma, mu gihe yagumye afise urugero rukomeye rw’ikigereranyo, canecane biciye ku gufatanya kwayo n’itegeko (nomos).



Ubwa nyuma, ukwaguka kw’ibiceri vyihuse birashingira intahe ihinduka rikomeye ry’imibano ya kera, aho gushiramwo amategeko y’agaciro k’amahera vyagendana n’imitunganirize ya Leta. Iryo hinduka ryashizeho umushinge w’ubutunzi n’ivya politike wo gutera imbere kw’ibihugu vya demokarasi vy’Ubugiriki, cane cane i Atene, aho amahera yari afise uruhara runini mu gukora kw’igisagara ca demokarasi.



Iciyumviro nyamukuru co kwibuka muri iki gice ni uko turiko turavuga cane cane **ibiceri**, atari amahera muri rusangi. Umuce nyamukuru ugaragara neza ni uwo **ukwizigira ubuyobozi butanga**, ufitaniye isano n’ibiranga ubuhinga bw’ibiceri (uburemere, ubusuku, agaciro k’imbere). Ukwo kwizigira nyene ni kwo gutuma Leta canke ubuyobozi butanga ivyo bice bishobora kugira urugero runaka rwo kugenzura canke mbere no gukoresha nabi agaciro k’ivyo biceri be n’ingene bigenda kuva mu ntango.




## Ingingo z'inzego n'ibiceri vya mbere


<chapterId>3e1efd08-99e3-5a32-9908-3185fef0e640</chapterId>



:::video id=84847cf6-9e46-4a8c-9f35-25a27496cc4b:::

### Kamere y'amahera ibiri



Kuza kw’amahera y’ubuhinga bwa none biravyura ikibazo nyamukuru: amahera yoba ari ikintu kiremwa n’isoko canke ni ikigo gitegetswe n’ubutegetsi? Ukwo guhuzagurika kw’ivyiyumviro gutuma habaho iyerekwa ribiri ritandukanye cane.



Ku ruhande rumwe, ishure ry’ubutunzi ryo muri Otirishiya riburanira iciyumviro c’uko amahera y’ibicuruzwa - cane cane inzahabu - yatowe mu buryo busanzwe n’abakozi b’ubutunzi kubera kamere zayo z’imbere: ugukomera, ugutwara, ugugabanywa n’uguhinduka. Uvuye muri ivyo, Leta yaciye yifatanya n’ayo mafaranga yihuta kugira ngo igenzure ukuntu atanga. Ni ikigo kiva mu bisanzwe mu bikenewe n’isoko imbere y’uko gifatwa n’ububasha bwa politike.



Mu buryo butandukanye n’ubwo, iciyumviro c’abahinga mu vy’imico kama n’inzego z’ubutegetsi kivuga yuko amahera abaho vy’ukuri biciye ku biceri vya Leta. Ubutegetsi bworemye ayo mafaranga buzi neza mu gushiramwo ikidodo cayo, gutyo bugahindura ico cuma kikaba igikoresho nyakuri co gukoresha amahera. Ivyo vyerekana ko ibiceri vya kera vy’i Lidiya vyakoreshwa canecane mu kuriha ingabo - stater imwe ihuye n’umushahara w’umusi w’umusirikare.



### Inyungu zidasanzwe z'ugushinga urugero rwa Leta



Naho hariho iyo ntambara y’ivyiyumviro, mbere n’abahinga mu vy’ubutunzi bo muri Otirishiya baratahura ivyiza bimwebimwe biva ku kwivanga mu vy’amahera Leta. Gushiramwo ibintu bimwe bimwe biciye mu gukora amabuye y’agaciro biratorera umuti ingorane zitari nke z’ubudandaji zikora.



Iyo ata bubasha bwo kwemeza, abakinnyi b’ubutunzi bahora bashikirwa n’ingorane: ibiceri vy’ibinyoma, ubuhendanyi bwo gutanga amakuru n’ugukoresha nabi uburemere. Ivyo bikorwa biratuma haba uguhuzagurika mu bukungu, kuko ibiceri bimwebimwe vyemerwa mu gihe ibindi bikankwa. Mu vy’ukuri, ikidodo cemewe kiratanga icemezo c’uburemere n’uburyo, bigatuma ubudandaji bugenda neza.



Ico kimenyamenya gifise igiciro kigaragara kw’isoko: igiceri c’inzahabu gicuzwe gifise agaciro kuruta igiceri c’inzahabu y’agaciro. Iryo shirahamwe ryerekana agaciro k’icemezo - abacuruzi ntibagikeneye kwisuzuma bonyene ko ico cuma ari ic’ukuri biciye mu bipimo vy’imiti canke vy’ijwi. Intambara ya Leta, mu buryo buteye ubwoba, irakuraho ugushihana kandi igatuma ubudandaji bworoha mu gutuma habaho ukwizigirana gushingiye ku nzego.



### Gukoresha nabi amafaranga kuva mu ntango



Inkuru y’abanyagihugu ba mbere bo muri Lidiya irerekana ikintu giteye isoni giteye ubwoba. Ivyigwa biherutse gukorwa vyerekana ko inzahabu iri muri ivyo biceri vy’umuyagankuba yari hasi cane kuruta iyo mu biceri vy’umuyagankuba kamere. Ubuyobozi bwemeza uburyo bwariko burakoresha icarimwe igihimba.



Ico gikorwa kirerekana akamaro kabiri k’amahera y’ibiceri. Ku bijanye n’isoko, bituma ubucuruzi bugenda neza kandi bitanga icemezo co guhuza ibintu. Ku buyobozi butanga, buca buba igikoresho co kugenzura ubutunzi biciye mu guhindura amazi. Mu kugabanya inzahabu irimwo mu gihe Leta iguma ifise agaciro k’izina, Leta yongera neza amahera - igatuma habaho amafaranga menshi avuye mu rugero rumwe rw’ivyuma vy’agaciro.



Ariko rero, Leta ubwayo yagumye ihagaritswe umutima n’ukwo gukoresha nabi abantu. Nk’uko vyerekanywe n’akarorero k’inzahabu solidus ya Constantin yo mu kinjana ca 4, ubutegetsi bw’Uburoma bwarasuzuma neza ukuntu ibiceri vyari vyiza, kuko vyasaba ko bihembwa mu biceri vyiza. Ubutegetsi bwari bufise inyungu ihambaye mu kubungabunga uburyo bw’ibiceri vyabwo bwite kugira ngo bubone agaciro k’amahera bwaronka mu misoro.



### Isesengura ry'ubutunzi ryo gutakaza agaciro



Ukwiga ibijanye n’ugucika kw’agaciro k’amafaranga birerekana uburyo buhoraho muri kahise. Ku biceri vy’ivyuma, abahinga mu vy’ubutunzi barakurikirana ijana kw’ijana ry’ivyuma vy’agaciro biri muri ivyo biceri - igicapo kimanuka kigaragaza ko agaciro kagenda karagabanuka. Ku mahera y’impapuro yo muri iki gihe, ni ibihushanye n’ivyo: amahera agendagenda araboneka, kandi iyo yiyongera, bigaragaza ko agaciro kayo gacitse.



Ubwo buryo bwompi bupima ikintu kimwe c’ishimikiro: ugusenyuka kw’agaciro k’amahera. Yaba mu kugabanya ivyuma vy’agaciro birimwo canke mu gucapura amanoti mashasha, uburyo bwo kubikora buraguma ari ubwo nyene. Uko ubutegetsi burema ibice vy’amahera vyinshi bivuye mu bintu vy’ukuri bimwe, ni ko n’igice kimwekimwe cose gitakaza agaciro kaco.



Ukwo gukoresha nabi, kugaragara mu biceri vya kera cane vy’i Lidiya, vyerekana yuko ukugenzura amahera kwamye ari ikibazo c’ububasha. Amahera akozwe rero agereranya ubuhinga bushasha budasanzwe bufatanijwe n’igikoresho co kugenzura ubutunzi - ububirigi bugenda mu mateka yose y’amahera, gushika n’ubu.



## Gukora ibice


<chapterId>b205f4f2-c293-5308-b812-a998de9ad45e</chapterId>



:::video id=47c612ec-d97e-4498-b50e-7e66518bd56d:::

### Kuva ku bipfunsi gushika ku biceri vyacuzwe



Inyuma y’igice kivuga ku guseruka kw’ibiceri, nashaka gutanga igice kigufi cane kivuga ku gutera imbere kw’uguhingura ibiceri. Nk’uko twabibonye, ​​vyose vyatanguye n’ibipande vy’umuyagankuba, bica bigendana n’inzahabu n’ifeza, aho impande zompi zari zishirwako ikimenyetso c’igipfunsi, haba mu maso h’umwami, canke umwobo mu mugongo kugira ngo umuntu asuzume ko ataco akora.



![image](assets/rn/008.webp)


Mu nyuma, nk’uko tuzobibona mu kigabane gikurikira, Abagiriki baranonosoye ubwo buhinga mu guhingura ibiceri vy’ibiceri vy’ikibumbano vyari bikubitwa n’inyondo ku mpande zompi. Baca bafata igice c’icuma c’agaciro kiryoshe kandi gisongoye, bagacapa ku ruhande rumwe igishushanyo bipfuza, hanyuma bakagitera inyundo n’ukuboko kugira ngo bareme ico giceri giheza.


Ubuhinga bwo gucapura ibiceri n’amaboko umuntu ku giti ciwe birashoboka ko bwagize uruhara mu kugenzura ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro muri ico kiringo, naho nyene akenshi ivyo biceri vyari bifise amazi menshi kugira ngo bibe vyinshi. Ivyo vyagaragaye canecane mu kiringo c’Abaroma, no ku rugero rutoyi, mu gihe c’intambara zimwezimwe zo mu kiringo c’Abagiriki. Naho gucapura ibiceri bimwe bimwe vyagabanya ubushobozi bw’ubutegetsi bwo gukora ibiceri vyinshi, vyarafashije cane mu kugenzura ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro, naho nyene hariho ugucika intege gukomeye kw’agaciro. Gutyo, ubwihindurize bwarateye imbere buva ku gipande c’icuma cariko kirakubitwa gushika ku gice c’ifeza c’ikibumbano kandi gicubitwa n’inyondo.


![image](assets/rn/009.webp)



### Ubwihindurize bwo mu kinjana ca mbere


Mu kinjana ca mbere, hariho kandi umugenzo wo gukwiragiza ibiceri, bikaba bikomeye kandi bike. Imvo imwe yatumye ivyo bishika ni uko vyaciye vyoroha kugerageza ijwi ryavyo, ivyo bikaba vyari bikoreshwa kenshi nk’ikimenyetso c’uko ari ivy’ukuri. Mu gukwiragiza iyo feza, vyatuma habaho incuro zitandukanye, ku buryo abantu bashobora kwemeza ko ico gice c’ifeza cari gisukuye mu kucwumviriza gusa. Uwo mugenzo niwo wavyaye ijambo "amahera meza". Mu bijanye n'amahera meza, uburemere busanzwe bwamenyekana hakoreshejwe umunzane canke "trebuchet" yo gupima. Gutyo, ubwihindurize bwarabandanije kuva ku biceri bitobito vy’ikibumbano gushika ku biceri vy’agaciro gatoyi kandi vyagutse.


### Gukubita kw'ipendule


Ubuhinga bwa nyuma bwashitse mu mpera z’Ikinjana ca mbere, mu ntango z’ikinyejana ca none, bwari iciyumviro co gutera ivyuma bita pendule. Yari ubwoko bw’ivyuma vy’ugukubita bikomeye kugira ngo bikubite ibiceri, gutyo bikaba bivamwo ibiceri bifise ubwo buryo bushasha bwo gukubita. Ico cari speaicl kuri iyo nzira ni ubushobozi bwo gucapura igicapo ku ruhande rw’igiceri kugira ngo umuntu ashobore gutorera umuti ikibazo co gucapura. Gucapura vyari birimwo gukuraho igice c’ico giceri kugira ngo umuntu asubire kuronka ifeza y’agaciro, iyo feza ikaba yari gushobora gukoreshwa mu gukora ibindi biceri canke gusa bikaguma ari ikintu co gukoresha.


Rero ico ciyumviro co gutera pendulum carafashije mu bijanye n’ugucapura. Kandi biraryoshe kubona ko iyo tekinoloji mu vy’ukuri yavuye mu Bufaransa. Nk’akarorero, mu Bwongereza, barahaye akazi abahinga b’Abafaransa kugira ngo baze kubereka ingene bakora izo mashini. Igiteye umunezero, ni uko hari abashigikiye uguhingura inyundo bari babirwanya kandi bacereje gukoresha ubu buhinga. Mu buhinga bwiza ubwo ari bwo bwose, hama hariho abantu baburwanya, bashaka kuguma bafise ubuhinga bwa kera. Naciye nibwira ko ari ubusazi cane gutahura ko mbere n’ubuhinga busa n’ubusumba ubundi vy’ukuri - ushobora gukora ibice vyinshi, biragoye kwigana - hariho abantu bakiriho bafatanye n’uburyo buzwi cane bw’inyondo. Hariho uguhinduka hagati yo guhingura ibihimba vyakozwe n’ico gitero kizwi cane c’ipendule hanyuma bagasubira ku gutera inyundo. Kandi mu nyuma, birashoboka, ni pendulum striking yaje gufata maze ikaduha ibi bice vyiza vy’ubu aho ushobora gusanga canke uturongo dutoduto, uturongo dutoduto dukikuje kugira ngo wirinde gukata, kumbure bifitaniye isano n’ijambo gukata, uturongo, kandi urashobora kubona n’ubu canke uturongo canke inyandiko canke ibishushanyo vyanditswe ku bice biri muri e.



# Ivyiyumviro bitandukanye ku bijanye n'uguseruka kw'amahera


<partId>72ac694f-9248-550d-90c1-91af3d234380</partId>




## Ivyiyumviro ku bijanye n'uguseruka kw'amahera n'insobanuro zayo zitandukanye .


<chapterId>7d699d4d-8c70-55b5-bf36-609f3fd90bcf</chapterId>


:::video id=523c873f-501b-4954-b79f-7e74c0f685a5:::

Murakaze muri iki gice kijanye n’inyigisho zitandukanye ku bijanye n’uguseruka kw’amahera n’insobanuro zayo zitandukanye. Ehe rero igice gitoyi co mu gitabu *Aux origines de la monnaie*, nibwira ko gicapura ivyiyumviro bibiri nyamukuru tuzoba turiko turaraba muri iki gice.



> Iyi ntangamarara ngufi nta yindi ntumbero ifise atari ugushira ahabona ivyerekeye ubushakashatsi. Ku rugero rw’ivyiyumviro, impaka zirafunguye hagati y’abashigikiye inyigisho ya K. Polanyi n’abashigikiye ivyiyumviro vya M. Weber. Ku ba mbere, ingabirano n’ugusubira gusangira birafise uruhara runini, aho uguhindura isoko bifise uruhara rutoyi gusa, cane cane mu guhindura mpuzamakungu. Ku bandi, ahubwo, isoko ni ryo riri mu mutima w’ingendo y’amateka iriho ubu.

Nk’akarorero, muri Mezopotamiya, inyigisho imwe y’uguseruka kw’urusengero ivuga yuko urusengero, nk’ubukuru, ari rwo rurema igice c’ibarabara canke igice c’amahera, rikagitegeka, hanyuma abacuruzi bakagifata kugira ngo bakore ubudandaji. Iciyumviro gihushanye n’ico kivuga ko, oya, iyo nkuru y’amahera isohoka mu buryo busanzwe mw’isoko kugira ngo yorohereze ubudandaji. Hariho ingero z’ivyo zishingiye neza muri Mezopotamiya.



Naho ku bijanye n’uguhinduranya, hari inyigisho zivuga ko vyakoreshwa cane cane mu guhanahana amakuru mpuzamakungu, ni ukuvuga n’abantu tutari twizigira.



Ivyo rero nivyo tuzokora muri iki gice. Tugiye gukora ubushakashatsi bumwe bumwe kugira ngo tugaragaze inyigisho zitandukanye ku bijanye n’uguseruka kw’amahera n’insobanuro zitandukanye z’ico amahera ari co. Tuzoba turiko turashikiriza no kunegura ivyiyumviro vy’abahinga mu vy’ubutunzi n’abahinga mu vy’imico kama. Nzogira mbere amahirwe yo kuba turi kumwe na Ulrich Fromy, azobabwira ivyiyumviro vy’umuhinga mu vy’ubutunzi wo muri Otirishiya kuri ivyo bintu bitandukanye.



## Uguseruka kw'amahera ku bahinga b'ubutunzi ba kera


<chapterId>1d3776cd-0dfd-5297-af48-c6f41e257a7e</chapterId>



:::video id=873a16c1-17ac-448d-8941-df4feb7ab79d:::

Iki gice kijanye n’inyigisho zitandukanye zijanye n’uguseruka kw’amahera. Ingingo ya mbere izokwihwezwa ni ukuza kw’amahera nk’uko abahinga mu vy’ubutunzi ba kera babivuga.



### Ivyiyumviro vya kera vya Adamu Smith



Dushingiye ku vyiyumviro vya kera vy’ubutunzi, cane cane ivyo vyashigikiwe na Adamu Smith, amahera yava mu guhinduranya amahera mu kwishura ku mipaka yayo. Mu ntango, uguhanahana kwakorwa biciye mu guhinduranya ataco akora, ariko ubwo buryo bwari bugoranye kenshi kubera ingorane y'"uguhuza kabiri kw'ivyo umuntu yipfuza»: umuntu wese yategerezwa kuba afise neza na neza ivyo uwundi yipfuza. Buhoro buhoro, ibicuruzwa bimwebimwe (nk’umunyu, ivyuma vy’agaciro n’ibitungwa) vyaje kwemerwa na bose nk’uburyo bwo hagati bwo guhinduranya, kubera akamaro kavyo, ukuramba kwavyo n’ukuntu bishobora kugabanywa. Gutyo, amahera yarabonetse ubwayo yorohereza no gutuma ubutunzi bugenda neza.



### Gunegura inyigisho za kera



Ehe rero ivyo nsubiramwo iyo nyigisho. Kubera ivyo twabonye vyose mu gice ca mbere, mbona ko dushobora kuvuga ko iki ciyumviro c’uko **ibiceri** ari ugutera imbere kw’uguhinduranya ari ikinyoma kubera gusa ko igiceri gicuzwe kiva ata kabuza mu butegetsi, kuko gicuzwe n’ubukuru. Hariho imvo zitari nke zituma ivyo bishika, n’icipfuzo c’abategetsi co kugenzura ubutunzi, co gufata amahera.



Ku rundi ruhande, nimba turiko turavuga amahera nk’iciyumviro, atari ngombwa ko ari ibiceri, rero ntaco bimaze kuko, n’ibiceri vya mbere, aba Lidiya staters, twabonye ibiceri vy’ifeza bitagira ikimenyetso. Hasigaye kumenya nimba zari ziriko ziragendagenda. Iyo ziriko ziragendagenda, ivyo bisigura ko abantu bashobora kuba baramenye mu ntango ko ico kintu ari amahera yoshobora gusabwa cane kandi akahindurwa bitagoranye. Kandi kumbure niho abategetsi babonye ivyo bintu, bakabifata mu kuvyishirako ikidodo kugira ngo bavyemeze.



Hariho ivyiza vyinshi mu gukora ivyo - ntaco bimaze kubisuzuma, kubipima, ivyo vyose. Biragaragara ko ivyo tuzobivugako. Ariko mu vyiyumviro vyanje, ibiceri biragaragara ko ari igikoresho cakoreshejwe n’ibihugu kuva mu ntango. Ariko ku bijanye n’uguseruka kw’amahera nk’uko ari, ntituzi nimba vy’ukuri yavuye ku butegetsi bwayategetse canke nimba yaserutse biciye mu bucuruzi canke mu guhanahana amakuru. Nzogira ikiganiro gishimishije cane kuri iyo nkuru n’uwo dukorana Ulrich mu nyuma muri iki gice.



Turamaze kumenya yuko ibiceri vya mbere vy’agaciro vy’icuma bitakoreshwa kugira ngo umuntu ashobore guhindura amahera ku musi ku musi kubera ko agaciro kavyo kari hejuru cane. Turazi kandi ko ahanini zakoreshwa mu kwishura abasirikare. Ivyo ni imvo nziza y’ivyo vyiyumviro vy’uko amahera atari ngombwa ko ava mw’isoko. Ivyiyumviro vy’amahera, ni ukuvuga amafaranga y’ibiceri vya mbere, birashoboka ko vyari binini cane ku buryo, nk’akarorero, umuntu yoshobora kugura umukate canke gukora ivyo gusuma ku musi ku musi. Nk’akarorero, vyoshobora kuba bingana n’umushahara w’umusi umwe. Si ngombwa ko abantu bahembwa umushahara muri iyo misi, ariko ivyo ni ukugira ngo ubone iciyumviro c’urugero. Ivyo biceri rero birashoboka ko vyari bifise ubushobozi bwo kugura vyinshi cane ku buryo vyari gukoreshwa mu bucuruzi butobuto. Ku rundi ruhande, ntaco twovuga ko ivyo bice vy’amahera bitazoba vyakoreshejwe mu guhindura ibintu binini cane, nk’ivyo abacuruzi bahindura. Turazi ko ahanini zakoreshwa mu kwishura abasirikare. Ivyo ni bimwe mu vyiyumviro bikundwa cane vyo gusigura ukuntu ibiceri vya mbere vyabonetse. Ibuka ko aha turiko turavuga ibiceri, si ngombwa ko tuvuga amahera muri rusangi. Rero, ibiceri vya mbere vyari bifise uruhara rwavyo rwa mbere, kandi urwo rwari urwo kwishura amahera y’igisirikare, y’abacangero.


Nk’akarorero, Alegizandere Mukuru yarakoresheje cane, nk’uko tuzobibona mu nyuma.



Twarabonye kandi ko kuva mu Bushinwa bwa kera, ibikoko vy’ibisiga vyakoreshwa mu guhindura ubutunzi (**guhemba abakozi, gupima agaciro no kugura ubutaka)**. Ikindi, muri Mezopotamiya no muri Misiri, uburyo bw’amahera bukora bwari busanzwe buriho kandi bwakoreshwa mu bucuruzi, mu kwishura umushahara no mu kwishura imisoro. Ico ndiko ndasaba hano ni uko ata gukeka ari bibi kwiyumvira ko ibiceri mu vyiyumviro vy’Abanyaburaya biva ku nkenegwa yo gutuma uguhanahana amakuru guhinduka.



Kubera ko ibiceri bisohorwa n’ubutegetsi, kumbure twokwiyumvira yuko, kuva mu ntango, vyari bifitaniye isano n’ubutegetsi bwabisohoye. Ivyo birafise insiguro. Ku rundi ruhande, ntitumenya neza ingene ubwoko bw’amahera canke ubwoko bw’imirongo y’amahera, ni ukuvuga ibiceri vy’intango, vyabanjirije. Ku ruhande rumwe, tugiye gutanga iciyumviro c’uko insengero ari zo zamenyesheje izo nzira z’amahera, hanyuma, abantu bakazikoresha. Kandi, ku rundi ruhande, tuzobabwira, oya, ni abacuruzi bari bakeneye uburyo bwo guhinduranya, uburyo bwo gucuruza n’isi yo hanze, kandi ni bo bamenye, nk’akarorero, icuma c’ifeza, co gukoreshwa kuko cari gikenewe n’isi yo hanze. Iciyumviro ni uko mu vy’ukuri tutazi. Ni co gituma dufise izo nyigisho zibiri zihushanye. Nta kimenyamenya gitunganye dufise co gusigura nimba amahera ava mu buryo busanzwe mu gukenera gucuruza, nk’akarorero n’abadandaza, canke nimba ava mu bukuru.



### Gutandukanya ibiceri n'amahera ya kera



Mu gusozera, mbona ko twovuga ko ibiceri biva ku bubasha ata kabuza, kuko vyashizweko ikidodo n’ubwo bubasha. Ku rundi ruhande, ntabwo mbona ko twovuga ko ari bibi gutanga iciyumviro c’uko amahera (ayo yabanjirije ibiceri) atashobora guseruka kugira ngo yorohereze uguhinduranya. Ngira ngo mu ngero zose twabonye haruguru, ingero muri iyo nsiguro ziragwiriye.




## Inkuru z'imigani zo guhinduranya


<chapterId>0fcd4964-ac36-5163-a8cf-1aacebc0d2c0</chapterId>


:::video id=0ede29ab-8acd-4d79-9282-bd5991b97076:::

### Isubiramwo rya Dawidi Graeber



Twarahejeje gupfuka ivy’uguseruka kw’amahera nk’uko abahinga mu vy’ubutunzi ba kera babivuga. None tugiye gutorera umuti iciyumviro kizwi kw’izina ry’imigani y’uguhinduranya.



Ikintu kimwe co kunegura iyo nyigisho ya kera y’uko amahera yaserutse ni ukubura ibimenyamenya vy’akahise bishigikira ivyiyumviro vyayo.



Ivyo bimenyetso vy'ugunegura bizwi kw'izina rya "barter myth", vyateguwe n'umuhinga mu vy'imico kama David Graeber, n'abandi, birarwanya iciyumviro ca kera c'uko amahera yavuye mu guhinduranya. Dushingiye kuri iyo nkuru y’ugunegura, nta kimenyamenya c’amateka canke c’ubuhinga bw’abantu kigaragaza ko imiryango yakoresha mu buryo butunganye ubuhinga bwo guhindura ibintu imbere y’uko amahera aza. Nkako, amashirahamwe ya kera yari gukora ashingiye ku ngurane, ku myenda, ku nshingano z’imibano no ku guhinduranya imigirwa. "Imigani y'uguhinduranya" rero ni inyubakwa y'ivyiyumviro yagenewe gushingira intahe iyerekwa ry'ubutunzi rya kera, ata shingiro nyaryo ry'ivyashikiye abantu.



Ariko rero, birakenewe kumenya ko iyo nyigisho idahakana ko hariho uguhinduranya, nk’akarorero, ku bijanye n’uguhinduranya hagati y’imiryango itandukanye. Rihakana gusa ko uguhinduranya ibintu vyari igikorwa gikorwa cane muri iyo migwi yitwa ko ari iya kera, kandi ko amahera yoba ari ugutera imbere kw’ivyo bikorwa mu buryo bubereye. Irahakana ko uguhinduranya ibintu vyakoreshwa cane mu muryango, kandi ko amahera amaherezo yava kugira ngo ahindure ibintu bibe vyiza no gutorera umuti ingorane zariho mu bijanye n’uguhinduranya ibintu. Ahubwo, hakurikijwe iyo nyigisho, iyo migwi yakoresha uburyo bwo gutanga inguzanyo canke ingabirano ku yindi.



### Imibano ya kera n'ubutekerezi bukomeye



**Ehe ibisobanuro bimwebimwe ku bijanye n’ubuhinga bukomeye bwa kera.** Ngira ngo iyo nyigisho ikora ata gukeka ku migwi y’abantu ba kera (batagira igihugu) bo mu bihe vya kera no muri iki gihe (nk’akarorero, imiryango yigishijwe n’abagenzuzi bo mu kinjana ca 18 n’ica 19). Biragaragara ko batakoresheje ubuhinga bwo guhinduranya, ahubwo bakoresheje uburyo bwo guhinduranya ivyo navuga, kubera imvo twamaze kuvuga (ugusangira ibikorwa bigoyagoya, uburimyi bwo kwibeshaho). Ariko rero, ntabwo mbona ko iyo nyigisho ikora ku mateka akomeye ya kera, nka Mezopotamiya na Misiri ya kera.



Aha hari ibice bibiri bivuye mu gitabu *Aux origines de la monnaie* ku bijanye n'iyi nkuru:



> Ico citegererezo cavuzwe na M. Mauss mu gitabu ciwe kizwi cane citwa "Ingabirano" carafashwe n'abahinga mu vy'ubuhinga bwa Misiri n'ubumwe n'igishika nk'uko nyene ata gutahura. Ivyo vyatumye habaho ibizazane vyinshi, ivyo ntituzovyinjiramwo ngaha. Reka tubone gusa ko iyo nzira yerekeye imibano yitwa ko ari iya kera, ivyo bikaba bitari vyo mu Misiri ya Farawoni.


> Imikate, ni ukuvuga intete zitunganijwe, rero zari ibice vy’ibara, nk’uko shât (y) y’Ubwami bwa kera, na vyo nyene vyashoboza gufungura inguzanyo mu bicuruzwa bitandukanye. Aka karorero koroshe karerekana yuko ubutunzi bwa Misiri ya Farawoni butashingiye ku rutonde rwo gusubira gusangira gusa. Vyari bigoye cane, vyari birimwo uguhanahana amakuru vyinshi.

Rero, nk’uko twabibonye mbere mu gice kivuga kuri Misiri mbere na Mezopotamiya n’Ubushinwa, turashobora kubona ko mbere n’izo ntara za kera, ariko zitari izo mu ntango, kubera ukubaho kwa Leta, mu vyiyumviro vyanje, zakoresha uburyo bw’amahera. Ngira ngo ivyo vyarerekanwe neza mu gice ca mbere c’iri shure. Kandi rero, ico ciyumviro co gutanga no kwakira, co gusubiza inyuma inguzanyo, ntikijanye n’izo mateka akomeye. Imvo nyazo zatumye amahera aza rero ziguma ari ikinyegezwa. Ntituzi nimba vyavuye mu gukenera abacuruzi gucuruza n’isi yo hanze, canke nimba vyategetswe n’urusengero muri ivyo bihe vya kera.




## Uguseruka kw'amahera biciye mu mafaranga y'imyenda .


<chapterId>4f508615-aa61-5d62-89d3-cecd02aeaa62</chapterId>



:::video id=a23f547f-3906-4f4a-8f72-5d78c649d0c4:::

### Amahera nka IOU



Muri iki gice, turavuga ku ciyumviro c’amahera y’imyenda.



Iciyumviro c’uko **amahera y’imyenda**, categuwe cane cane n’umuhinga mu vy’ubutunzi Alfred Mitchell-Innes, hanyuma kigashirwa mu ngiro na David Graeber, kivuga ko amahera atavuye mu guhinduranya, ahubwo ko yakomotse ku migenderanire y’imyenda n’inguzanyo yariho kuva mu mibano ya kera y’abantu. Dushingiye kuri iyo nyigisho, amahera aboneka iyo inshingano zo mu kibano (imyenda hagati y’abantu canke imigwi) zicitse zigereranywa kandi zikaba zishobora kwimurirwa. Ico ciyumviro kizana iciyumviro c’ugupima igitigiri c’ibintu bihindurwa n’ivyo kwimurirwa. Gutyo, amahera yoba ari hejuru ya vyose **ukwemera umwenda**, ashigikiwe n’ukwizigirana kandi akenshi ashigikiwe n’ubukuru bwa politike canke bw’idini, aho kuba igicuruzwa gikora gusa nk’umuhuza mu guhinduranya.



Uburyo bumwe mbere buteye imbere kuruta bw’ico ciyumviro ni uko amahera yose ari umwenda. Rero umuntu afise amahera yoba afise ikirego ku kibano muri rusangi, ikirego ku bemera ayo mahera bose. Kandi ko amahera, **mu vyo babona, ategerezwa kwemerwa mu buryo bw’agahato**, ahandi ho si amahera, kuko iyo ushobora kwanka ayo mahera, systeme yabo ntikora. Mu mugwi watanzwe wamenye amafaranga, abo bose bayafise, ni nk’aho bafise umwenda ku bandi bose bo muri iyo sosiyete bemera ayo mafaranga, kandi abemera ayo mafaranga bafise uburyo bw’umwenda ku muntu afise iyo nkuru y’amahera. Ivyo ni vyo mu vy’ukuri vyiyumviro vyabo.



### Gunegura uburyo bw'inguvu



**Ivyo negura kuri iyi nyigisho:**



Reka nkore ikintu kimwe gitoyi co kunegura iyo nyigisho. Ndemera ko amahera ari ubwoko bw’uguhuriza ku bantu. Ni icizigiro umugwi ushira mu "kimenyetso" c'amahera, uko coba ari kwose. Rero ndashigikiye iciyumviro co kwizigirana, ico tuzosubira kugifata mu nyuma n’iciyumviro c’amahera y’imbere. Aho bigorana ni igihe abashigikiye iyo nyigisho bongerako iciyumviro c’inshingano bagashimika ku ciyumviro c’imyenda. Kuri bo, iyo umuntu afise token y’amahera, aba afise ikirego ku kibano cose, kandi rero ikibano coba gifise umwenda ku muntu afise. Hazoba kandi itegeko ryo gutorera umuti, abagize umugwi bakabwirizwa kwemera token; ahandi ho, mu kubona kwabo, iyo nzira ntiyokora. Ngira ngo uburyo bwavuzwe haruguru mu Bushinwa bwa kera buraserukira neza iyo nyigisho.



Ku ruhande rwanje, ndashobora kwiyumvira bitagoranye uburyo aho amahera ari ukwiyumvira kw’abantu aho token yatowe yemerwa muri rusangi nk’uburyo bwo kwishura, ata n’itegeko ry’itegeko. Nshobora kubona urutonde nk’urwo rukora iyo abantu bavyemeye ku bushake bwabo. Bishobora gukora. Ku rundi ruhande, akenshi bizanana n’inshingano, amafaranga yemewe n’amategeko, n’ubukazi, ivyo tuzobibona mu nyuma mu kigabane. Ariko mu vy’impwemu, nta ciyumviro mfise c’uko iyo nzira ishobora gukora neza. Ngira ngo Bitcoin ni akarorero. Bitcoin irafise agaciro kuko ifise amahera y'imbere, kuko hariho ugusaba ko ikoreshwa mu mafaranga, ni ukuvuga, ibisigazwa vy'agaciro, kumbure n'uburyo bwo guhindura canke gukingira uburyo bwa fiat. Nta n’umwe ategerezwa kuvyemera, kandi uko vyemerwa nk’uburyo bwo kwishura, ni ko bishobora gukoreshwa nk’uburyo bwo guhindura. Turashobora gusa kuyikoresha nk’ububiko bw’agaciro ata ngorane. Nta nkeka kuri ivyo. Ico nshaka kuvuga ni uko Bitcoin isa n’akarorero kuri jewe, ubwoko bw’amahera ari uburyo bwo kwumvikana mu kibano aho twiyumvira ko tuzoshobora kugarura amahera yacu nitwagura amwe mu nyuma, tukayaronka kugira ngo dushobore kuyahindura mu nyuma, kugira ngo tuzigame ubushobozi bwacu bwo kugura.



Ukwo kubona ivyigwa bitagira aho bigarukira birafasha gusigura ingene imiryango ibiri itandukanye ishobora gucuruza n’amahera token nk’inzahabu, ataco irema canke umwenda hagati y’iyo miryango. Guhatira kwemerwa mu kibano, ndabona ko bidakora mu bucuruzi hagati y’imiryango ibiri, kuko uwundi muryango ntuyoborwa n’ubukuru. Umuryango B ntugenzurwa n’umuryango A. Ariko naho biri ukwo, yemera iyo token y’amahera nyene reka tuvuge, inzahabu. None, abantu boshobora kumbwira ngo "Ego, ariko ivyo ni kubera ko sosiyete B nayo yafashe ingingo y'uko inzahabu ariyo mafaranga yabo", rero birakora. Ego cane, birakora, ariko nta kurema umwenda kuri iyo nkuru. Ni ugucuruza kwa nyuma. Rero, iyo sosiyete A ihinduye ikintu n’inzahabu muri sosiyete B, nta kuremwa kw’imyenda kubaho, iyo nzira y’ugucuruza iraheza. Kandi biragaragara ko uwo muntu ari mw’ishirahamwe B ataronse ico gice c’inzahabu canke ico gice c’inzahabu kugira ngo mu nyuma kizohembwa n’abantu bo muri ishirahamwe A. Aremera ko bamuhindura inzahabu. Aremera ko azoyihindura mu nyuma, kumbure mu muryango wiwe bwite. Rero, muri aka karorero, nta kurema umwenda, nta n’ikirego gihishijwe, ni uguhinduranya gusa, ukwishura ataco bimaze. Abashigikiye amafaranga y’imyenda bazotubwira ko ivyo ari uguhinduranya. Kandi jewe ntavyemera, kuko uguhindura ni uguhindura ikintu ciza kitaziguye. Guhindura ibintu ataco bimaze ni uguhindura ikintu kimwe n’ikindi, kugira ngo gikoreshwe. Ibintu birahindurwa kugira ngo bikoreshwe, mu gihe muri twebwe, inzahabu ikoreshwa neza nk’amahera kuko nta kindi izokoreshwa mu gukora; nivyo bizokoreshwa mu nyuma nk’uburyo bwo kwishura. Rero, mu vyiyumviro vyanje, ntibishika mu rwego rw’uguhinduranya.



Kugira token y'amahera si "ugusaba" ku kibano, ahubwo ni icizigiro c'uko token izokwemerwa mu nyuma ku gaciro kagereranywa.



## Ukwibonekeza kw'amahera


<chapterId>e3ef86b1-73b9-5140-a61e-2ab6a5b0b2d4</chapterId>


:::video id=e543995f-d5e2-49d7-9133-e397b46e0833:::

Ku mashure y’ubutunzi yo muri Otirishiya, yatangujwe na Carl Menger, amahera ava mu buryo busanzwe mu bukungu bw’uguhinduranya ibintu buhanganye n’ingorane y’uguhuza kabiri kw’ivyo umuntu ashaka. Muri iyo mbonerakure, abantu bihuza ubwabo ku bicuruzwa vyo hagati bishobora kworohereza uguhinduranya - atari ibicuruzwa bikoreshwa ataco bimaze, ariko ibicuruzwa vyemewe kubera ubushobozi bwavyo bwo gusaba cane.



Ivyo bintu vy’amahera bitegerezwa kuba bifise kamere zamenyekanye kuva kuri Aristote: bitegerezwa gukora nk’ububiko bw’agaciro, uburyo bwo guhinduranya n’igice c’ibarabara. Abakozi b’ubutunzi barabimenya buhoro buhoro, bakabirundanira kandi bakabizigama, gutyo bagatangura guseruka nk’amahera. Ivyo vyose biva ku vyo umuntu akora - amahera aserukira inyishu y’isoko ry’akameremere ku ngorane yo guhuza ubucuruzi, ata n’ubutegetsi bugira ico bukoze.



### Impaka z'"inkuru z'imigani"



Abahinga mu vy'imico kama nka David Graeber barahakana ivyo vyiyumviro, bavuga ko ari "inkuru z'imigani y'uguhinduranya". Iciyumviro cabo: nta n’iterambere rikomeye rishingiye gusa ku guhinduranya ibintu ataco rihinduye ryigeze ryandikwa. Ahubwo, imiryango ya kera yigishijwe yakoresha uburyo bwo gutanga inguzanyo zidasanzwe no gusubizanya. Graeber yemeza yuko umwenda wabanjirije uguhinduranya, akavuga ibipande ibihumbi n’ibihumbi vyo muri Mezopotamiya vyerekana imigenderanire y’inguzanyo.



Ariko rero, ivyo binegura bishingiye ku nsobanuro y’uguhinduranya ibintu. Nk’uko Menger yabivuze mu 1892, uguhinduranya ibintu birenze uguhinduranya ibintu ataco bimaze. Birimwo kandi n'uguhindura amafaranga, ibikorwa vy'imishahara, n'uguhinduranya amafaranga y'igihe gito - ivyo Menger yise "uguhindura amafaranga hagati y'abantu". Ubwo buryo bwagutse bwo guhinduranya burashobora kubana n’uburyo bwo gutanga inguzanyo mu migwi y’ukwizigira.



Kubura ikimenyamenya si ikimenyamenya c’ukubura, kandi abahinga mu vy’ubutunzi bo muri Otirishiya baremera ko ata kibano gikomeye gishobora gutera imbere mu buryo buramba gishingiye ku guhinduranya ataco bimaze gusa - ni co gituma bikenewe ko amahera aza.



### Ivyabaye muri Mezopotamiya: abacuruzi n’insengero



Ivyo biganiro biriko biratera imbere ku bijanye n’inkomoko y’ishekeli y’ifeza yo muri Mezopotamiya. Hariho insobanuro zibiri zitandukanye. Iciyumviro c’inzego kivuga ko insengero - ibibanza vy’ukuri vy’ubutunzi n’ivy’impwemu - vyashizeho ifeza nk’amahera yo gutunganya ubutunzi. Ivyo bipande vy’inyuguti z’inyuguti, vyari vyibanze cane ku bakuru b’idini no ku bacuruzi b’abanyacubahiro, birashingira intahe ukwo kugenzura kwari gushizwe ahantu hamwe.



Insobanuro y’Abanyaotirishiya ivuga ibihushanye n’ivyo: abacuruzi ni bo bafata amahera yo gucuruza kure. Kubera ko bari bahanganye n’ingorane yo gucuruza n’abanyamahanga bari hirya y’imipaka ya Mezopotamiya - kuva muri Anatoliya gushika mu Kiyaga c’Ubuperesi - bari bakeneye ikintu cemewe kw’isi yose, kizomara igihe kirekire kandi gishobora gutwarwa. Ifeza yari ihitamwo ry’akameremere kubera kamere zayo z’imbere. Insengero zaremeje gusa umugenzo wari waramaze gushingwa n’ugukoreshwa mu vy’ubudandaji.



Iyi nyigisho ishingiye ku nyandiko z’uguhanahana amakuru hagati ya Kanesh muri Anatoliya na Assur, aho abacuruzi bahinduranya impuzu n’ivyuma vy’ifeza - atari kubera akamaro kavyo k’ibintu, ahubwo nk’ububiko bw’agaciro. Ivyo bicuruzwa vyarenze uguhinduranya gusa, bihishura ukubaho kw’amahera y’ibicuruzwa vy’ukuri.



### Akarorero k'ubu k'amakambi y'imbohe .



Umuhinga mu vy’ubutunzi yitwa Richard Radford, uwari imbohe mu Budagi mu gihe c’Intambara ya Kabiri y’Isi Yose, yaranditse ikintu giteye umunezero c’uko amahera yaje kwibonekeza. Mu makambi, itabi ryacitse mu bisanzwe ikintu co guhinduranya - kigabanwa, gihuye n’ivyo umuntu ashaka, cemerwa na benshi. Mbere n’abatari abanywa itabi barazifata, bamenya ko zifise agaciro ko guhanahana amakuru kw’isi yose.



Iyi microcosme yerekana ingingo ngenderwako y'Ubudagi: iyo umuntu ahanganye n'ingorane yo guhuza ubucuruzi, abantu baca bahuriza hamwe ku ciza "gishobora kugurishwa" kuruta ibindi vyose. Nta butegetsi bwategetse amahera y’itabi; ryavuye mu ngeso ya misi yose y’infungwa zirondera gutuma ibintu bigenda neza.



### Uguhuza kw'ivyo umuntu akunda



Mu vy’ukuri, amahera agereranya uguhuza ivyo umuntu akunda kugira ngo aronke inyungu rusangi yemewe. Abacuruzi bo muri Mezopotamiya, cokimwe n’infungwa za Radford, barabonye ivyiza vyagabanya ukudakeka kw’uguhinduranya ibintu muri kazoza. Ukwo guhitamwo ntikurindira kwemererwa canke gutegekwa n’ubutegetsi bukuru - kuva ku ntumbero y’ibikorwa y’abakozi b’ubutunzi bahanganye n’ingorane z’uguhinduranya.



Impaka hagati y’uguseruka kw’ibintu n’inzego z’ubumenyi ziguma zifunguye, kuko ibimenyamenya vy’akahise ari ibice bikeyi. Ariko isesengura ry’Abanyaotirishiya ritanga insobanuro ihuye: amahera yavutse bivuye ku bikenewe vy’ubudandaji, abategetsi bagashira gusa mu nzego imigenzo yari yaramaze gushingwa n’ikoreshwa ry’isoko.



## Iyerekwa ry'abahinga mu vy'imico kama ry'uguseruka kw'amahera


<chapterId>ec48c5d8-47ed-530f-beb7-c44fd0b62880</chapterId>


:::video id=8c1f8764-75af-4fb6-a98b-55de3b7da02e:::

### Inkomoko y'amahera idashingiye ku bukungu



Muri iki gice, turatohoza ukuntu abahinga mu vy’ubuhinga bw’abantu babona ivy’uguseruka kw’amahera, uburyo buhambaye butera ingorane cane inyigisho za kera z’ubutunzi.



Mu buryo butandukanye n’ivyiyumviro vya kera vy’uko amahera yavutse mu buryo busanzwe mu guhinduranya ubutunzi kugira ngo bishobore gutuma habaho uguhinduranya ubutunzi, ubushakashatsi bwakozwe n’abahinga mu vy’imico kama bwerekana ko ukuza kw’amahera ahanini gushingiye ku bintu bitari ivy’ubutunzi. Biva ku buryo bwo mu kibano nk’ugutanga amakori, indishi y’ubwicanyi (Wergeld izwi cane) n’inkwano (amahera y’umugeni), ariko kandi biva ku migirwa, idini, politike n’imigenzo y’ikigereranyo, birenze kure n’iyo ivy’isoko vyoroshe.



Mu mibano ya kera, amafranga ntiyakoreshwa cane mu guhinduranya ibintu, bitandukanye n'insobanuro ya kera y'amahera nk'"uburyo bwo guhinduranya". Nkako, ayo mashirahamwe yarakoresha cane inguzanyo, n’ugusubiramwo amahera bishizwe mu nzira nini z’imigenderanire y’abantu n’iy’abantu ku giti cabo. Ivyo bikoresho vy’inguzanyo vyari hose, mu buryo bubereye kandi bushingiye ku mateka, vyabanjirije amahera kuboneka.



Ivyo ni vyo bicapura iyerekwa ryabo. Ivyo turabiganirako na Ulrich mu kiganiro cacu co muri videwo iheruka. Nzoreka mwinovore ivyo Ulrich yavuze ku bijanye n’ico kibazo, bikaba bitera urujijo gatoyi iyo nzira. Kandi rero, mu vyo yerekwa mu vy’ubuhinga bw’abantu, kenshi turagira ico ciyumviro c’uko amahera ava ku butegetsi canke iciyumviro c’imibano kibanziriza ivyo isoko rikeneye.



### Akarorero k'amabuye y'i Yap .



Aha musi, urashobora gushima akarorero gatangaje k’amabuye y’agaciro yo mw’izinga rya Yap. Amwe muri ayo mabuye, naho ataco akora canke mbere akabura ku mubiri, yarabandanije gukora neza nk’amahera biciye ku masezerano rusangi, ivyo bikaba bishimika ku rugero nyamukuru rw’amahera rwerekeye imibano n’ikigereranyo.



![image](assets/rn/010.webp)



Ivyo ni vy’ukuri isesengura riryoshe cane ry’amabuye y’i Yap. Saifedean Ammous na we nyene aravuga ako karorero mu gitabu ciwe "Itegeko rya Bitcoin". Nk’uko yabivuze, uburyo bwo ku kirwa ca Yap busa cane na Bitcoin, ubwoko bw’inyandiko nyamukuru umuntu wese ashobora kuraba, ni ukuvuga iya bose, icungera amakonti no gucunga uburenganzira bw’ibintu. Ukwo kubona ibintu mu vy’ubuhinga bw’abantu kwerekana ko ivyo vyose bigereranya amasezerano canke ukwiyumvira kw’abantu mu kibano, ivyo bikaba ari ukuri mu vy’ukuri. Kandi mbona uku kuvuga amabuye yazimiye gushimishije cane. Baca baja mu kiyaga amajana y’ibilometero mu mato mato mato, bagaca bazana ayo mabuye. Rimwe na rimwe iryo buye ryagwa mu mazi yo mu kiyaga, ariko iryo buye ryari kuguma rikoreshwa mu bijanye n’amahera. Umuntu yovuga ati: "Ego, twatereye ibuye ahantu nk'aho; ni iryanje, kugira ngo turihindure". Ntiyari ngombwa ko umuntu agira ivyo afise kugira ngo ashobore guhinduranya, kuko ayo mabuye yari manini cane ku buryo kenshi yaguma ahantu hamwe. Ahubwo, ikintu nyamukuru cari uguhindura amaboko n’ayo mabuye mu buryo bw’ugucuruza, bikaba vyatuma ubutunzi bushobora guhinduka ata mabuye yimuka vy’ukuri. Yari uburyo bw'"ikimenyamenya c'uguhurizako", bugaragaza uburyo bushimishije bwo kubona amahera mu vy'ubuhinga bw'abantu.



### Amafaranga y'intango n'inshingano z'imibano



Abahinga mu vy'imico kama kw'isi yose barabonye imiryango ikoresha "amafaranga y'intango" canke "amafaranga ya kera", nk'ibikoko, impuzu, amatungo, umunyu, n'amabuye, ivyo bikaba vyarangura ibikorwa bikunze gushirwa ku mafaranga, nk'uburyo bwo kwishura n'ububiko bw'agaciro buri musi, ata however.



Rero, aha turiko turadondora uburyo bw’amahera butakoreshwa vy’ukuri mu guhinduranya amahera ku musi ku musi.



Kandi ndashaka kubibutsa ko ayo yose yari amafaranga imbere y’uko haza ibiceri, kandi sinzi ingene ari izina ribi kuvuga amafaranga. Nkunda kuvuga amafaranga. Nshobora kuvuga ko mu bitabu, kenshi tuvuga amafaranga y’intango kugira ngo tuvuge amahera imbere y’ibiceri. Ariko nk’uko twabibonye mu gice ca mbere, **Nizera ko hariho uburyo bw’amahera kera cane imbere y’uko ibiceri biboneka**.



Aya mafaranga y’intango yakoreshwa canecane mu gucungera inshingano z’ishimikiro zo mu kibano zifitaniye isano n’abantu ku giti cabo, nk’ubugeni, indishi y’amatati (Wergeld), canke ingabirano hagati y’abakuru. Nk’akarorero, mu Bwami bw’Ubuperesi, ibiceri vya mbere vyaremwe mu buryo budasanzwe kugira ngo bibe uburyo bwo kwishura ingabo aho kuba uburyo bwo guhinduranya.



Amahera y’intango rero arafise ikintu kimwe nyamukuru kiranga: ni uburyo bwo kwishura, ariko gake cane ni uburyo bwo guhinduranya ibintu vy’umubiri ata guca ku ruhande. Ico dushaka kuvuga aha ni uko bwari uburyo bwo kwishura inshingano zimwe zimwe zo mu kibano, imiryango, uguhanahana hagati y’abakuru, wergeld izwi cane, amahera y’amaraso. Imbere y’uko ubutungane buza, iyo umuntu yishe umuntu, hariho indishi ku muryango wababajwe n’ukwica uwo bakunda. Hariho igiciro co kwishura ivyo, vyitwa amahera y’amaraso kandi ni uburyo bwo kwishura. Hariho kandi n’inkwano, na yo nyene ni uburyo bwo kwishura. Muri ivyo bikoresho vya mbere vy’amahera nk’uburyo bwo kwishura, vyari bifitaniye isano cane n’inshingano z’abantu n’iz’imibano kuruta kwishura ivyo bagura ku musi ku musi. Dushingiye kuri iyo nyigisho, ivyo bintu vyari bimenyerewe cane ku musi ku musi vyari bifitaniye isano cane n’inguzanyo, inguzanyo yasubitswe, ingabirano ku yindi, no gusubira gusangira ibifungurwa. Hariho ubundi buryo bwo gutunganya imibano kugira ngo ivyo biganiro bishobore gucungirwa. Ni vyiza kandi kwibuka ko, mu kibano aho umuntu wese yitunga, akora uburimyi bwiwe, ata n’umwe yizeye, kandi ko ata n’umwe akeneye uburyo bw’amahera bwo guhindura ibintu ku musi ku musi. Kandi ni co gituma uburyo bwa mbere bw’amahera bwari ubwo twahejeje kudondora, inkwano, amahera y’amaraso, kubera gusa ko ayo yari amahinduka ya mbere aho twari dukeneye uburyo bwo kwishura, kera cane imbere y’uko dukeneye gucuruza, guhindura umukate n’amahera ku musi ku musi, kuko mu mibano ya kera, ntivyagenda gutyo. Umuntu wese yarironsa ivyo akeneye, kandi nta n’ubuhinga bwihariye bwariho. Ngira ngo ivyo narabivuze cane mu nyigisho zose zabanje muri iri shure.



Muri ivyo bihugu, ata gucapura kw’ibikorwa kwari guteye imbere, uguhanahana ataco bimaze vyaguma ari bike, bikaba vyabaye ahanini mu migenderanire y’abantu ku giti cabo y’ubugenzi canke y’ubumwe. Kuba ata buhinga buhagije bwari buhari ntivyasaba amahera mu buryo bwa none.



Abahinga mu vy’imico kama nka Quiggin na Einzig bashimika ku vy’uko inguzanyo ari yo ibanza: **ubuzima bw’ubutunzi bwa kera bwafashwe n’uruzitiro runini rw’inguzanyo n’imyenda y’umuntu ku giti ciwe, aho amahera yinjira cane cane iyo amahera ategerezwa kwishurwa ubwo nyene kandi indishi zidashobora gusubirwamwo bitagoranye.**



Rero, abantu barahindura ibintu, bashobora gutanga inguzanyo isubitswe, ariko mu bihe bimwe bimwe, ntushobora gusubiza inyuma kwishura, rero amafaranga canke amafaranga y’intango arashobora kuba ngirakamaro muri iki gihe kugira ngo ugire iherezo ry’uguhinduranya.



### Ubuhinga bushasha bwo kutamenyekana



Iryo sesangura rituma umuntu yiyumvira cane: aho kurwanya amahera ngo ahindurwe, birabereye cane gutahura ukuntu yaserutse nk’uguhinduka kuva ku mice igoranye y’inguzanyo n’imyenda. Amahera azana ubuhinga bushasha bw’ishimikiro: **ukutamenyekana**. Kandi niho mbona iyo nyigisho y’ubuhinga bw’abantu y’uguseruka kw’amahera iryoshe cane. Nimba muri umugwi mutoyi w’abantu kandi mukahana deferred credit, biragaragara ko mumenyana. Ngira ngo kugira ngo iyo nzira ikore, abantu bategerezwa kumenyana, biragaragara. Kandi ukwishurwa n’amahera bituma umuntu atamenyekana. Bigufasha kwishura ata bantu mbere bazi izina ryawe, ata bantu mbere bazi uwo uriwe. Bashobora gukora uguhinduranya kugira ngo bashobore gutorera umuti ibibazo vy’ubu nyene kandi vy’iherezo. Kandi ivyo ni vyo nyene amahera ashoboza.



Mu buryo butandukanye n’inguzanyo, iyo na yo yama ari iyo gutanga izina, amahera arashoboza gukora ibikorwa bitamenyekana, bihurikiye hamwe kandi bihita bibohora. **Ubwo bubasha bwihariye bwo kwidegemvya bw'amahera ni bwo busumba ubundi bwose.**



Gutyo, aho kuba igikoresho gisanzwe co kworohereza uguhanahana ubutunzi, amahera ni ikintu gishasha mu kibano, gifitaniye isano cane n’ugutera imbere kw’inzego n’imigenzo y’abantu, kuva ku ngurane z’umuntu ku giti ciwe **gushika ku buryo bwo kwishura rusangi, butazwi**. Iryo terambere ry’ubuhinga bw’abantu ryerekana ko amahera, atari kure cane y’uburyo bworoshe bwo guhinduranya, aserukira ikigo gikomeye c’imibano, gihingura cane imibano y’abantu, ku buryo mu mibano yacu ya none, aba ari yo ntumbero nyene y’ibikorwa vy’ubutunzi.



Aha, turatahura ko mu mpera, mu mibano yacu ya none, intumbero nyene y’uguhinduranya ubutunzi ari ukugira amahera, mu gihe kera, ivyo ntivyari bimeze na gato. Intumbero nyene y’uguhanahana ubutunzi yari iyo kugira ibintu canke ibintu vyo gukoresha. Kandi uno musi, mu gushiramwo ubuhinga bushasha bw’amahera, intumbero y’uguhinduranya ubutunzi ni ukwirundanira ayo mahera, kuko adushoboza kuyahinduranya ivyiza, nk’uko vyemerwa muri rusangi. Turashobora kubihindura ivyiza dukeneye igihe tubikeneye.



## Kwandika ubumwe


<chapterId>7664442a-91c1-5ce4-a8bd-53b7371a3e3d</chapterId>


:::video id=473fc284-5375-4e1b-b0cd-6b51ba0cc3b8:::

### Ivyiyumviro vy'inyandiko y'ivy'itunganywa ry'amafaranga



Ubu tugiye gutohoza hamwe ivyiyumviro bitandukanye vyo guhuza izo nyigisho zibiri z’amahera, ni ukuvuga, inyigisho y’uguseruka kw’amahera biciye mu myenda-amahera n’inyigisho y’amahera y’uguseruka kw’amahera y’ibicuruzwa. Tugiye kuvuga ku ciyumviro ca Lynn Alden co guhuza abantu mu gitabu ciwe kizwi cane citwa "For Broken Money", umutwe w'ubuhinduzi bwaco bwakozwe na Consensus kumbure uzokwitwa "Rupture monétaire".



*Igice c'igitabu c'amahera yavunitse canditswe na Lyn Alden:*



> Mu vy’ukuri, amahera ni igitabu c’ivy’ubuhinga. Amahera y’ibicuruzwa ni igitabu kigenzurwa n’ibidukikije. Amahera ya banki ni igitabu kigenzurwa n’ibihugu-bihugu. Amahera yuguruye ni igitabu kigenzurwa n’abakoresha bayo.

Aha, Lyn yerekeza kuri Bitcoin.



### Igipimo c'ububiko n'ubukene



> Ibintu bimwebimwe vy’imiti bidasanzwe, nk’akarorero rhodium, biraboneka cane kuruta inzahabu, ariko birafise igitigiri gito c’ibintu bishobora gukoreshwa kubera ko bikoreshwa n’inganda vyihuta nk’uko bicukurwa. Igiceri canke igice c’ibara ry’agahama gishobora kugurwa nk’ikintu kidasanzwe co gukoraniriza hamwe canke ububiko bw’agaciro, ariko ntikibereye nk’amahera yemerwa n’abantu, kandi rero ntigisohoka mu buryo busanzwe nk’amahera.

Saifedean arabivuga cane mu gitabu ciwe "Itegeko rya Bitcoin". Ku batazi igipimo c’ububiko n’ububiko, ni gusa iyo ugereranye ububiko buriho, ububiko buri kw’isoko, ugereranye n’ububiko bushasha buriko buraza, ukwinjira kw’ububiko bushasha. Kenshi na kenshi birahushanye n’ivyo umuntu abona, kuko woshobora kwiyumvira ko ikintu ufise mu bwinshi kitari gito, ariko mu vy’ukuri si ko biri. Ni ikibazo c’ubushobozi ufise bwo kuyitanga. Ahubwo ni ubushobozi dufise bwo kugira ububiko bushasha, hakurikijwe iki kigereranyo, buduha amakuru y’uko ico kintu ari gake canke atari co. Si kubera ko ataco dufise mu bubiko ari gake, ni kumbure gusa ko tutagifise. Rero, nitwafata inzahabu, turafise inzahabu nyinshi kuko zikoreshwa nk’ububiko bw’agaciro, kandi ukwinjira kw’inzahabu nshasha ni nk’ibice 1% gushika kuri 3% ku mwaka vy’inzahabu nshasha yinjira biciye mu nzahabu mining. Ariko, ivyo ariko aravuga hano, nimba turiko turavuga ivy’i rhodium, irake cane kuruta inzahabu, ariko nta stock dufise kuko irafungurwa uko igenda. Ntibisaba rero ibintu vyinshi bishasha kugira ngo umuntu akure kabiri ivyo yari afise. Ariko ku bijanye n’inzahabu, vyofata n’imiburiburi imyaka 50 kugira ngo ivugururwe, kugira ngo ivy’ubutunzi bibe bibiri. Udakunze ibicuruzwa vyinshi bikoreshwa, aho vyoroshe cane, kandi ntibifata imyaka myinshi kugira ngo umuntu akure kabiri ivyo afise, kuko bikoreshwa uko bigenda.



*"Inzahabu yagumye ifise igipimo c'ububiko n'ubucuruzi kiri hagati ya 25x na 100x muri kahise k'ubu, akenshi hafi 50x canke irenga, mu gihe gitoyi ntiyigeze igwa munsi ya 16x, mbere no mu gihe c'Ikigobe c'Inzahabu co hagati mu kinjana ca 19. "*



Rero, 25 vyoba bisobanura imyaka 25 kugira ngo umuntu akubye kabiri ivy’ububiko, 100 na vyo bikaba bisobanura imyaka 100 kugira ngo umuntu akubye kabiri ivy’ububiko. Saifedean avuga mu gitabu ciwe ko naho twokubita kabiri inzahabu, kuva ku 1,5% gushika ku 3%, ntivyogira ingaruka nyinshi ku giciro cayo.



*"Ifeza muri rusangi ifise igipimo c'ububiko c'ibice 10 canke birenze, ivyo bikaba bikiri vyinshi cane.*


*Ibindi bicuruzwa vyinshi bifise igipimo c'ububiko kiri munsi ya 1 canke 2. Mbere n'ibintu bidasanzwe, nka platine na rhodium, birafise igipimo c'ububiko buke cane kubera ko bikoreshwa vyihuta mu nganda."*



### Ubusumbasumbane bw'inzahabu n'ifeza .



*"Muri make, igihe cose amafaranga y'ibicuruzwa yisanze ariko arahiganwa n'inzahabu n'ifeza, ayo mafaranga yama asohoka hejuru mu mpera. Ibindi bicuruzwa vyoshobora kuguma ari amafaranga mu bihe bike canke mu turere twihariye, ariko inzahabu n'ifeza vyama vyerekana ubushobozi bwavyo bwo kuba amafaranga ahanganye kw'isi yose iyo bihuye n'amafaranga y'igihugu. inzahabu n'ifeza vyama bifise ubushobozi bwo guca agaciro k'ubundi buryo bw'amahera, mu gihe abafise ibikoko, amasaro, amatungo, umunyu, impuzu canke ivyuma vy'agaciro gatoyi batashobora kwigera bagabanya agaciro k'inzahabu canke ifeza."*



Ivyo rero birasubirwamwo neza cane muri The Bitcoin Standard aho Saifedean avuga ku miryango yo muri Afirika yakoresha amabuye y’ibirahuri. Kandi igihe abacuruzi b’i Venise bashika bafise imizigo yuzuye amabuye y’ibirahuri kuko bari bashoboye kuyahingura mu nganda ico gihe, bari bafise ubushobozi bwo kubikora, vyatumye uburyo bw’amahera bw’ivyo bihugu buhungabana rwose kandi barashobora gusahura ubutunzi bwabo vy’ukuri. Ivyo ni vyo Saifedean yavuga.



### Igice ca konti n'inguzanyo



*"Mu mateka, mbere n'igihe inguzanyo yakoreshwa ataco ihinduye nk'igikoresho co guhindura, akenshi yakoreshwa mu bice vy'ibicuruzwa vy'amahera vyatoranijwe mu buryo busanzwe kubera imitungo yabo."*



Ico ni iciyumviro gishimishije cane, kandi ni co jewe na Ulrich twama tuganirako. Naho urusengero rwo muri Mezopotamiya rwari ubwoko bw’ubukuru bwashobora gucungera ico ciyumviro c’inguzanyo, igipimo c’ibara cari shekeli. Ntaco cemeza ko shekeli yashinzwe n’urusengero. Shekeli yari gushobora guseruka mu buryo busanzwe, biciye ku nkenegwa y’abadandaza yo kwinjiza no gusohora n’abandi bantu bo mu karere. Turafise ibimenyamenya vy’ivyo, mu buryo bw’umucuruzi wo muri Kanesh (ivyo nabivuze mu Gice ca 1) yakoze ivyo nyene, akazana ivyuma vy’agaciro bitakoreshwa kubera agaciro k’ibicuruzwa vyavyo vy’umubiri, ahubwo nk’ububiko bw’agaciro. Ikibazo conyene ni uko tutazi nimba twokwiyumvira ko iyo nzira yo guhitamwo ifeza, y’ifeza shekeli, yakozwe n’abadandaza, canke ko yakozwe n’urusengero. Ariko Ulrich afise imvo nziza cane ituma twiyumvira ko kumbure ahubwo ari ku ruhande rw’abadandaza ari ho yakozwe.



*"Rero, ubumwe bw'izo nyigisho zibiri burashobora kudondorwa nk'"inyigisho y'ubuhinga bw'amahera" ("inyigisho y'amahera") kuko idondora ivyiyumviro vy'ishimikiro bihurikiyeko izo nyigisho zompi. hagati yabo kugira ngo ntibaze bahaze ivyipfuzo bibiri bihuye, bagabanye ugushihana mu guhinduranya, kandi bikore nk’uburyo bwo kuzigama amahera Itandukaniro ry’ingenzi riri mu bubasha bwajejwe kubika igitabu c’amazina."*



Ku ruhande rumwe, kamere ni yo igenzura ukwaguka kw’amahera. Rero, nitwafata inzahabu, nk’uko ari gake cane, biragoye kuyicukura. Hariho ubwoko bw'umupaka w'ibiceri vy'inzahabu bishobora gucukurwa. Rero ubukene burongorwa n’ibidukikije. Kandi igitabu c’ivyandika gifatwa n’iciyumviro c’ugutunga. Igitabo c’ivyandikano kirashizwe ahantu hamwe. Ugutunga bigaragazwa n’uko ufise igiceri c’inzahabu canke igice c’inzahabu. Kandi ku bijanye n’amahera y’inguzanyo, ubukene bugenzurwa n’ubushobozi bw’abantu bwo kuronka inguzanyo. Canke ku bijanye n’amahera ya fiat, ubukene burongorwa n’ubukuru. Ni bo bafata ingingo yo gucapura vyinshi canke kutabicapura, kugira ngo ntihagire ivyago vy’ugutera imbere kw’ibiciro. Rero, mu bihe bimwebimwe, igitabu c’amazina gishobora kandi kurongorwa na nyen’igitabu ca token, ku bijanye n’amahera y’impapuro. Ni co gituma ryinjizwa mu gitabu, mu bimenyetso vy’ugusubiramwo, rikagira dematerialisation. Ego cane, ivy’umubiri, ariko vy’ukuri. Arafise iyi token izwi cane, kandi nivyo vyerekana ko afise. Kandi bishobora kuba vyoroshe cane mu gitabu nyaco, nk’uko biri ku mahera yo mu vyanditswe, muri banki, aho mu vy’ukuri ari banki y’abantu igenzura uwufise iki mu bijanye n’igitabu.



## Ubumwe biciye mu giciro c'amahera


<chapterId>093756e5-8908-55e5-bb76-376a3a3cc4d3</chapterId>


:::video id=eabc342a-ecbd-46ca-a347-e914917e7c4f:::

### Iciyumviro c'amahera y'imbere



Muri iki gice kijanye n’ivyifuzo bitandukanye vyo guhuza ivyiyumviro bitandukanye ku bijanye n’uguseruka kw’amahera, nca nshinga ivyiyumviro vya Lyn Alden, ivyiyumviro vy’inyandiko. Nfise iciyumviro canje co guhuza izo nyigisho zibiri z’amahera. Ni amahera y’imbere, iciyumviro c’amahera y’imbere. Rero, agaciro k’amahera gashobora gusigurwa n’amahera y’imbere akomoka ku vyo asabwa, haba mu buryo bw’ibipande vy’ibumba, ibiceri vy’icuma c’agaciro, amafaranga y’amahera, canke bitcoin. Ico kiguzi c’amahera gishingiye gusa ku cizigiro c’uko hari uwuzohindura ayo mafaranga muri kazoza ku giciro kigereranywa.



Ico ngerageza kwerekana hano ni uko gusa yaba ari fiat, ni ukuvuga amafaranga y’amabanki ataco amaze, yaba ibiceri vy’inzahabu canke icuma ico ari co cose, igice c’inzahabu canke igice c’inzahabu, **kenshi ni amahera y’imbere akora igice kinini c’agaciro kayo**. Iyo dufashe igice c’inzahabu, igice kinaka c’agaciro kayo kirasigurwa n’agaciro kayo ko gukoresha, uko ikoreshwa mu nganda canke mu gukora amabuye y’agaciro. Zirikana ko ugusaba amabuye y’agaciro kenshi biva ku gaciro kayo k’amahera. Abantu bagumya amabuye y’agaciro nk’ubwoko bw’ububiko bw’agaciro, rero ivyo ndabishiramwo gatoyi mu giciro c’amahera kuko kenshi ni ugusaba amahera kugira ngo umuntu agire uruhara mu mahera.



Rero wovuga ko hafi 10% vy’inzahabu isaba ari ivy’inganda. Mu gaciro k’inzahabu, twogira igice gitoyi, reka tuvuge 10%, ivyo vyoba bisigurwa n’ico gisaba c’inganda, ico gisaba co gukoresha inzahabu, aho inzahabu ikoreshwa. Ibindi ni ugusaba gutomoye ko ikoreshwa mu vy’amahera nk’ububiko bw’agaciro.



### Ubukuru bw'agashimwe na fiat



Kandi iyo ugereranye igice c’inzahabu n’igiceri c’inzahabu, hariho ikindi gice. Ico gice c’inzahabu gishirwako ikidodo n’ubutegetsi, kandi inzahabu iri muri ico gice na yo nyene irasabwa gukoreshwa, ni ukuvuga ko ikoreshwa mu nganda. Iraronka kandi amahera y’imbere nk’ububiko bw’agaciro. Ikindi, hariho igipfukisho nitwa authority premium, aho kenshi hazoba igiciro, ubushobozi bwo kugura igiceri kuruta igice c’inzahabu, kuko igiceri coroshe gukoresha. Bituma uguhanahana bigenda neza, kuko ata nkenerwa yo kubipima. Ubukuru mu bisanzwe buratanga icemezo c’ubusuku bwabwo. Kandi iyo ugereranije n’igice c’inzahabu, igiceri c’inzahabu giteye ikidodo muri rusangi kirafise agaciro kuruta igice c’inzahabu gisanzwe. Kandi ivyo navyo ni ibisanzwe, kuko bisaba ubutunzi kugira ngo umuntu abishireko ikidodo.



Ni ingingo imwe nyene ku mahera ya fiat, y’impapuro. Amahera y’impapuro ntaco amaze vy’ukuri, kiretse kumbure gushusha inzu, kandi ivyo vyabaye mu gihe ca Repubulika ya Weimar. Rero nta n'ivyo vy'ukuri bisabwa ku gaciro k'ikoreshwa ryayo. Kurundi ruhande, hariho gusa igiciro c’ubukuru, mu vyiyumviro vyanje.



Ni uburyo bw’amahera y’imbere, igipfukisho ku mahera y’imbere. Ariko amahera yayo y’imbere ava ku kuba ari amahera yemewe n’amategeko, hanyuma abategetsi bakaguhatira kuyigura kugira ngo wishyure imisoro yawe. Rero, vy’ukuri, amafaranga y’amahera afise uburyo bwo gusaba amahera buva ku kuba akoreshwa imisoro kandi utegerezwa nibura kuyaronka kugira ngo wishyure imisoro yawe. Kandi ivyo bituma riguma ari uburyo bwo kwishura bwemewe muri rusangi. Abantu rero barashaka kuyironka kugira ngo bashobore gushitsa ivyo bakeneye.



### Ubumwe biciye mu gusaba amahera



Kandi ni kuki iki ciyumviro c’amahera y’imbere gishobora kuba ari uguhuza inyigisho zibiri z’amahera y’imyenda n’amahera y’ibicuruzwa? Erega, sinzi ko agaciro k'igiceri c'inzahabu kava ku "gaciro kaco k'imbere". Oya, mu vy’ukuri, ni iciyumviro co kwizigira nk’uko biri ku mahera y’amahera. Ni iciyumviro c’ugusaba amahera. Kandi si kubera ko ifise igice gitoyi c'ikoreshwa ry'inganda, ikindi "gikoreshwa". Nitwavuga ko ikoreshwa ry’inganda ari 10% vy’agaciro karyo, ivyo twobiha agaciro ku madolari 300 ku ounce. Iyo inzahabu igurishwa kw’isoko ku madolari 3.000 ku nkoko, itandukaniro riri hagati y’amadolari 300 n’amadolari 3.000 ni ryo ry’amahera rizwi cane. Ni uku gusaba amahera kw’inzahabu nivyo bisigura. Kubera ko fiat ifise agaciro k’ikoreshwa rya zero ntibisigura ko itandukanye. Kuri jewe, ni co kimwe nyene. Rero ku mpande zompi, inyigisho y’amahera y’imyenda canke amahera y’ibicuruzwa, sinibaza ko ubwoko bw’uburyo bwongerekanye inzahabu yogira bwo kugira agaciro gatoyi k’ikoreshwa buhindura ikintu na kimwe.



Ku rundi ruhande, birazwi neza ko **ku rugero rw’uguseruka, hakurikijwe ivyiyumviro vya Mises vy’ugusubira inyuma, dushobora gusaba ko iyo nkoresha irema ugusaba ku ntango kandi igatanguza inzira ihinduka amahera.** Mu gihe, ku rugero rw’amahera y’imyenda, ari ugutegekwa n’ubutegetsi, rero the complete of the bitandukanye. **Ariko mbona ko ku rugero rw’agaciro, ingene twosigura agaciro k’amahera, n’amahera y’imbere, dushobora gusigura mu buryo bworoshe nk’uko nyene igituma amahera ya fiat afise agaciro tuyashirako n’igituma amahera y’ibicuruzwa afise agaciro** tuyashirako. Kuri jewe, ni iyo nzira nyene, kandi yitwa amahera y’imbere.



#### Igiciro c'amahera



Nivyo. Agaciro k’amahera gashobora gusigurwa n’amahera y’imbere akomoka ku vyo asabwa, haba mu buryo bw’ibipande vy’ibumba, ibiceri vy’icuma c’agaciro, amanoti y’amahera canke bitcoin.


Ico kiguzi c’amahera gishingiye gusa ku cizigiro c’uko hari uwuzohindura ayo mahera mu nyuma ku giciro kigereranywa.



![image](assets/rn/011.webp)



# Insobanuro zitandukanye z'amahera


<partId>77b7918a-8c3b-11f0-b688-6b2ab22378c9</partId>



## Amahera n'ifaranga n'amahera n'ifeza n'ugutegura


<chapterId>bf8a6d21-df88-5d23-a0a5-e9a5c1300554</chapterId>


:::video id=d9c9e7df-9db3-4a9f-801e-10d3fc7dfc22:::

### Insobanuro y'amajambo y'amahera



Muri iki gice kivuga ku vyiyumviro bitandukanye vyerekeye amahera na cane cane ku nsobanuro z’amahera, noshima gutanga insiguro ngufi ku ruhande ku bijanye n’insobanuro y’amajambo. Nashaka kwimba gatoyi mu nsobanuro z’amajambo menshi yerekeye amahera, nkayagereranya n’ayo mu congereza. Nk’akarorero, amahera, amafaranga, ugereranyije na monnaie, argent na devise. Rero, bigenda gutya.



Insobanuro ntoyi:



Iyo tuvuze "**amahera**" (de la monnaie), abantu benshi bazokwibaza ko turiko tuvuga ihinduka ritoyi turonka mu gusubiza igikorwa. Kandi iyo tuvuze "**amafaranga**" (la monnaie), abantu bazokwibaza ko turiko tuvuga amafaranga y'igihugu. Ifaranga rya Canada ni idolari rya Canada. Nivyo nyene.



Ariko none amahera (de l’argent) yoba ameze gute? Umusuma ntazokwigera avuga ngo "Mpa amahinduka yawe yose!" (uwo musuma yoshobora neza guhemuka iyo aronse ibiceri gusa hafi ata co bimaze).



Oya, umusuma azosemerera ati: "Mpa **amahera yawe yose**". Kandi iyo uwo musuma ahagaze imbere yawe mu nzira, aba ariko yerekeza ku **amafaranga** ari mu mufuko wawe.



Kurundi ruhande, iyo uwo musuma agerageza kuguhenda mu buryo buteye imbere cane, agerageza kwiba itunga ryawe mu gukuraho ubusa kuri konti zawe zose zo muri banki, twovuga ngo **azotwara amahera yawe yose**. Aha ijambo "amahera" ryerekeza ku **ubutunzi bw'umuntu ku giti ciwe**.



Rero hariho insobanuro zibiri z’ijambo amahera: amahera (amafaranga y’amabanki) n’ubutunzi.



### Amafaranga n'amahera n'ugutegura



Ifaranga (devise) ni ngombwa ko ari amafaranga y’ikindi gihugu, ahandi ho tuvuga gusa amahera (monnaie). Iyo uri umufaransa, wovuga uti: «Igihugu c’Uburayi ni co gitegekanijwe n’ukwezi kw’Uburayi» (Ifaranga ry’Uburayi ni ryo ry’Ubwongereza, euro ni ryo ry’Uburayi).



Kenshi, abantu batarashika kure muri izo ngorane z’insobanuro, mu guhindura ayo majambo, kenshi bazokunda kuvuga amafaranga (devise) iyo ari amafaranga yanditswe, ariko oya, amafaranga ni amafaranga (monnaie) iyo ari amafaranga y’igihugu cawe, kandi ni devise kuvuga amafaranga ayandi. Kandi rero, ingorane hano nkunda kubona ni uko mu congereza, hari amajambo abiri: hariho "amahera", ari co ciyumviro, kandi hariho "amafaranga", ari co mu vy'ukuri igice c'igihugu gikoreshwa mu guhinduranya. Rero turashobora kuvuga gusa ku ciyumviro c’amahera; biroroshe - ni iciyumviro c'ijambo *amahera*; ni amahera muri rusangi. Kandi *amafaranga* ni yoroshe cane kugereranya n'amafaranga y'igihugu. Ariko mu gifaransa, ikibabaje, abantu bazovuga kenshi ngo ego, "mais ce n'est pas une monnaie" iyo bavuga ivya bitcoin kuko atari amafaranga y'igihugu, ariko kenshi, mbona ko bariko bavuga amajambo amafaranga aho kuvuga amajambo amafaranga. Ivyo ni bibi ku ruhande rumwe, kuko kuva muri El Salvador, bitcoin ni yo yari amafaranga y’igihugu. Ikintu kiguma ari uko abantu bazovuga kenshi bati: *ariko oya, si amafaranga y’igihugu, ntashobora kuba amahera*. Ariko mu vy’ukuri, nitwavuga ku ciyumviro cagutse ca *amahera*, bitcoin irahuye neza cane n’iyo nsobanuro, mu vyiyumviro vyanje. Ni uko gusa mu gifaransa, ata majambo abiri dufise yo gutandukanya ivyo vyiyumviro bibiri. Twovuga ko ijambo argent ryerekeza ku mafaranga, ariko ikibabaje, iyo si yo nsobanuro yayo nyayo. *Argent* (amahera) yerekeza ku butunzi canke ku bipapuro vy'amafaranga. Ntushobora vy’ukuri gukora ikintu kingana n’ijambo *amahera*. *Amahera* ni vy'ukuri iciyumviro c'amahera (monnaie).




## Insobanuro ya Saifedeyani Amosi


<chapterId>07c4ba50-168c-567a-8957-0b187ff75f97</chapterId>


:::video id=936d6d3b-6d45-468e-bc44-85fbce9b857a:::

#### Amahera ni iki?



Amahera ni ikintu gusa ufise canke uronka kugira ngo ntukoreshe canke ngo ukoreshe kubera wewe nyene, ahubwo ngo uzogihindure mu nyuma n’ibindi bintu canke ibikorwa woba ukeneye. (Ikinyafede)


Amahera aronka inyungu y’amahera iyo hariho ugusaba amahera ku ciza, kugira ngo akore uruhara rumwe canke nyinshi z’amahera.


Ivyiza vy’amahera bitegerezwa kuba bike cane kugira ngo igiciro c’amahera kibeho (kugira ngo ugutanga ntiguhure n’ivyo amahera asaba).




### Igiciro c'amahera



Muri iki gice kivuga ku nsobanuro zitandukanye z’amahera, nashaka kuvuga muri make insobanuro ya Saifedean mu gitabu The Bitcoin Standard, kikaba cama kinshimisha cane. Vyankubitse nk’aho vyoroshe cane igihe nabisoma. Kandi tuzokwongerako n’iciyumviro c’amahera y’imbere muri iyo nsobanuro. Nk’uko Saifedean abivuga mu gitabu ciwe, hariho ata kabuza iciyumviro c’ubukene. Ikibazo ni iki, amahera ni iki?



> Amahera ni ikintu gusa ufise canke uronka, atari co co gukoresha canke ngo ukoreshe kubera co, ahubwo co guhindura mu nyuma ibindi bintu canke ibikorwa woba ukeneye.

Rero iyo ni yo nsobanuro Saifedean avuga mu gitabu ca Bitcoin. Nari kwongerako ko amafaranga (la monnaie) aronka amahera y’imbere iyo hariho ugusaba amahera ku ciza, kugira ngo akore uruhara rumwe canke nyinshi z’amafaranga. Wovuga rero ko ifaranga rikora nk’ububiko bw’agaciro rizogira igisabwa c’amahera kizoriha amahera y’imbere, kuko abantu bashaka kurironka, nk’akarorero nk’ububiko bw’agaciro canke nk’uburyo bwo guhindura amahera.



### Ubukene n'uburyo bwo gutanga isoko



Kuri ivyo, mbona ko dukwiye kwongerako ata gukeka ko ivyiza vy’amahera bitegerezwa kuba bike cane kugira ngo amahera y’imbere ashobore kubaho. Ivyo birahambaye cane. **Igihe ikintu kivuyeho kugira ngo gikoreshwe nk’amahera tukabona igiciro caco kiriko kiraduga, mu bisanzwe, iyo ico kintu kitari gito bihagije, abantu bazoshaka kugihingura vyinshi kugira ngo bungukire kuri iyo nyungu y’agaciro iyo igiciro kiduze**. Ni co gituma ibintu vyinshi biri kw’isoko bifise igiciro kidahinduka. Iyo igiciro kiduze, umusaruro urakunda kwiyongera. Iyo igiciro kigabanutse, umusaruro uragabanuka. Hariho ubwoko bw’uguhindura isoko. **Kandi iyo ikintu ari gito cane, nk’inzahabu, uburyo bw’isoko ntibuzosubiza inyuma ivyo bisabwa vyiyongereye vyo gukoresha amahera. Rero ni igihinduka gihinduka, ni igiciro. Nk’uko biri ku bitcoin**. Iyo igiciro ca bitcoin kiduze, ntidukora bitcoin nyinshi. Ico rero gihindura ni igiciro. Kandi ni co gituma, mu myaka, twabonye igiciro ca bitcoin kiduga uko abashaka bitcoin bagenda baraduga. Kubera ko ata n'umwe kw'isi ashobora guhindura ubuhinga akavuga ngo "hariho ivyifuzo vyinshi, igiciro kiriko kiraduga, tuzokora vyinshi." **Ugutanga ama bitcoins mashasha birategurwa imbere y’igihe, kandi biramenyekana imbere y’igihe**. Ivyo rero nivyo nariko ndavuga, ko ivyiza vy’amahera bitegerezwa kuba bike cane kugira ngo igiciro c’amahera gikomeze, kandi rero ntikifatwe n’uburyo bw’isoko, kugira ngo ugutanga ntibihure n’ivyo bisabwa bishasha vy’amahera.




## Uburyo bwo kwishura n'agaciro k'ukwibohora


<chapterId>5d424039-e342-56f7-9d8b-bba9551831a9</chapterId>


:::video id=af4c0765-8111-4cb7-891b-3ee54d6e7054:::

### Uburyo bwo kwishura n'uburyo bwo guhindura



Muri iki gice kijanye n'insobanuro zitandukanye z'amahera, ndasaba ko tworaba hamwe amajambo yasubiwemwo mu gitabu "Aux origines de la monnaie" (Inkomoko y'amahera), igisomwa ca Alain Testart ku bijanye n'amahera nk'uburyo bwo kwishura n'agaciro k'ukwibohora.



*Mu gitabu Aux origines de la monnaie, Alain Testart asigura ko amahera ari uburyo bwo kwishura:*



> Ibikorwa vy’uburyo bwo kwishura bifatwa aha nk’ibitandukanye n’ibikorwa vy’uburyo bwo guhindura, ku rugero hariho ukwishura ataco bimaze, ukwishura ataco kugura. Knies (1873:192 ff.) arategura cane iyo nsiguro y’ugutanga ibintu bitagizwe n’ibikorwa vyo guhindura, nk’uko biri ku vyerekeye wergeld (amahera y’amaraso canke igihimba c’ubwicanyi) canke imisoro. Carl Menger yateye iyo nzira ya kane mu kiganiro ciwe co mu 1892 citwa "Geld", muri rusangi kibonwa ko ari kimwe mu bifata ingingo cane kuri iyo nkuru. Hatariho gusenyuka rwose, iciyumviro c’igikorwa c’uburyo bwo kwishura gisa n’icabaye cibagiwe mu vyiyumviro vy’ubutunzi muri iki gihe, canke n’imiburiburi kikanka kugira ngo haboneke ic’uburyo bwo guhindura.
>


> Amahera akoreshwa mu kwishura: abonye muri ubwo buryo, ni igikoresho co kwibohora, kidondora muri rusangi igikorwa c’uburyo bwo kwishura. Muri ivyo, tuvuga "ububasha bwo kwibohora" bw'amahera. Nk'uko Le Petit Robert abivuga, ububasha bwo kwibohora ni "ubwo bufise ingaruka zo kwibohora (ku nshingano, umwenda)". Nk'uko bivugwa na Grand Larousse, ukwishurwa kw'ukwibohora ni "ukwishurwa kwose gukorwa hakurikijwe amategeko mu buryo uwufise umwenda adashobora guhakana ukuzimangana kw'umwenda". Amahera arafise ubwo bubasha par excellence; mbere ni co gisobanura ikibanza caco c’amahera, kubera ko ata n’umwe ashobora kwanka kwishura amahera, yaba uwugurisha canke uwugurisha. Amahera ni co ciza conyene kidashobora kwanka mu kwishura ivyo umuntu afise umwenda, ata kuraba ko uwo mwenda ari uwufitiye umucuruzi canke umukozi w’ikori. Mu bintu vyose, amahera ni yo yonyene afise ako gateka. Charles yanditse ati: “Ni ako gateka. Gide (1921 I: 443), ari ryo rigize ico twita amafaranga yemewe n’amategeko.
>


> Uguhindura kwose gushingiye ku kwimurira ikintu kimwe mu kindi, canke hakurikijwe ko ikindi kintu gitangwa mu gusubiza, bisobanura ata kabuza ko uwugihawe afise inshingano yo gutanga uwo mugenziwe. Kwishura ni ugushitsa iyo nshingano. Guhindura vyose rero bisobanura kwishura, ariko si ukwishura kwose bisobanura guhindura. Hariho ivyishyurwa ata n’umwe abisubiriza, ni ukuvuga ivyishyurwa bidatuma umuntu aronka ikindi ciza, kandi bitakorerwa iyo ntumbero. Imisoro iguma ari yo karorero k’ingenzi aha; dukwiye kandi kuvuga amande y’ubwoko bwose yishurwa inzego za Leta, n’indishi zifitiye abandi ku ngingo ngenderwako y’uko uwugiriye nabi abandi ategerezwa kubisanura.

### Ukwishura ata wuwufasha
